Important News

Central Government and National Government Memorial Week 67

Chen Zhaoying Reports on Inspection Trip to Fujian

Chairman Chiang Reports on Communist Suppression Military Affairs and Disaster Relief

▲At 9:00 AM on the 7th, the Central Party Headquarters held the 28th weekly memorial service for the Premier in the auditorium. Central Committee members Chen Zhaoying, Fang Juehui, Chen Lifu, Wang Boling, and others, as well as staff from various departments and guests, totaling about 500 people, attended. Wang Boling presided over the meeting. After the ceremony, Chen Zhaoying reported on his inspection trip to Fujian, stating that he had been ordered to go to Fujian twice, once to inspect Party affairs and once to inspect military affairs. He then briefly outlined his findings and thoughts. Regarding the shortcomings in Party affairs, he noted that most Party members only knew about ordinary work within the Party and did not pay attention to the necessary external movements. They only took on the Party's name, and were not very clear about the Party's responsibilities and all regulations. There was little contact between Party members and the public, their spirits were dispersed, and disagreements easily arose. As for the social aspect, the situation was very complex. Party officials only knew to generally reject bad and corrupt elements, and could not find ways to influence and correct them, making it difficult to eliminate reactionary forces and impossible to develop Party affairs. Regarding military affairs, whenever the Red bandits launched an attack, the Party headquarters and local people were extremely panicked and fled. Although there were civil defense organizations in various counties, their strength was weak. Furthermore, because the bandit suppression troops were sparsely distributed, it was difficult to lead various self-defense groups to mount a strong defense. Therefore, the bandits who fled from Jiangxi were able to wreak havoc in northern Fujian, and the local people suffered greatly. An investigation revealed that most of the bandits in Fujian were local bullies, with very few true Red bandits. When they first arrived, they preached communism, and many people were hypnotized by them. Later, they changed their faces, robbing, plundering, burning, and killing everything. By this time, even if the people wanted to resist, they could not. From this point of view, it was due to the failure to fully develop military efficiency, but more importantly, the Party headquarters and Party members had failed to effectively carry out the work of influencing and leading the people. Therefore, in the future, all comrades who handle Party affairs should take leading society as a prerequisite for their work, earnestly assume the responsibility of propaganda and training, and work hard towards the people. This is not only the case in Fujian, but all Party members in various parts of the country should understand this principle. The meeting adjourned after the report.

▲At 10:00 AM on the same day, the National Government held a weekly memorial service for the Premier. Chiang Kai-shek, Yu Youren, Zhu Peide, Ye Chucang, Wang Zhengting, Wang Boqun, Ma Fuxiang, Lian Shenghai, Zhou FoHai, He Yaozu, Lin Xiang, Ru Yuli, Wei Daoming, Chen Yi, Chen Shaokuan, Gao Weiyue, Zhang Wohua, and more than 300 staff members from the National Government's civil service, military affairs, accounting, and other departments attended. Chiang Kai-shek presided over the meeting. After the ceremony, Chiang reported on supervising the suppression of bandits and inspecting the flood situation, stating that the work of suppressing the Red bandits in Jiangxi Province had not slackened in the past two months. The soldiers at the front were enduring hardship, which was even more painful than that of the flood victims. Now, thanks to the efforts of the soldiers, the main force of the Red bandits has been defeated, and all bandit nests have been eliminated. This can be reported to the people. Rumors of failures in bandit suppression are all reactionary fabrications. Although there are still remnants of bandits fleeing east and west in Jiangxi Province, he is confident that if Guangdong does not obstruct them, the problem can be completely resolved soon. Recently, it has been reported that Guangdong and Guangxi have sent troops to the Chenzhou area of Hunan, hoping to take advantage of the Yangtze River flood and the imminent elimination of the Red bandits to confront the Central Government, collude with imperialists, and receive supplies of guns and ammunition. At a time when the Chinese people are washing away national humiliation, Guangdong is taking such actions, which shows that their conscience has been completely lost. Even if they were to win by chance, they would be spurned by the people, and the result would inevitably be failure. Regarding the flood problem, the disaster in Wuhan and northern Jiangsu is heartbreaking. Not only should government colleagues have a responsibility to alleviate the suffering of the people, but all citizens should also have this responsibility. We must work together with one heart to overcome this disaster and unite under the guidance of the Party to overcome this difficulty and maintain order. Next, he also expressed his views on the issuance of disaster relief bonds as follows: (At this time, when domestic and foreign troubles, natural disasters, and man-made disasters are pressing in, our Party comrades, entrusted with the heavy responsibility of the Premier, face the serious impact of the current situation. Only by being of one mind and one heart, with the spirit of abiding by the law, the determination to be responsible, and rushing towards the goal of saving the country and the people, can we overcome dangers and overcome great disasters. Zhongzheng has been on expeditions for months, and the order in the rear depends on the maintenance of the comrades in the Central Government, so that Zhongzheng has no need to worry about internal affairs and can concentrate on suppressing the Red bandits. This is not only what Zhongzheng personally appreciates, but also what the people of the whole country expect. The disaster relief bonds passed by the Legislative Yuan, with a total amount of 80 million, were passed by the Central Political Conference in full, without reducing it by a penny. The comrades of the Legislative Yuan are enthusiastic about disaster relief, and the Central Political Conference has never lagged behind. Moreover, there are currently no accurate statistics on the disaster victims in each province, and the disaster situation in each province is being actively investigated. If it is considered necessary in practice, the Central Government should continue to handle disaster relief by adopting all other effective methods in addition to issuing these bonds. This is the first point that Zhongzheng dares to report to the people of the whole country with responsibility. The Central Political Conference decided that the 80 million public bonds should be issued in installments, originally for the convenience of promotion, hoping to avoid losses of these public bonds in the market and reduce the actual benefits of the disaster victims. These public bonds are now decided to be issued in two phases. The first phase is 30 million, which will be issued within ten days, and before it is printed, the unused portion of the salt tax bonds issued last time will be fully advanced, and military and political expenses will be temporarily postponed. The second phase is 50 million, which will be issued before the end of the 20th year. This is the second point that Zhongzheng dares to report to the people of the whole country with responsibility. However, regarding the second point, I also hope that the Legislative Yuan will pass it as soon as possible. If it still insists on misunderstandings and makes it impossible to proceed with this case, the disaster victims who are on the verge of death will be greatly affected. Now, let me offer some contributions to the comrades on the nature and relationship between the five branches of the National Government, in the spirit of Party governance and the spirit of the rule of law: (1) The five branches exercise five powers, and these five powers are completely independent. However, the principle of independence has only one element: not to infringe on each other. For example, regarding the powers between the Legislative Yuan and the other branches, the comrades of the Legislative Yuan should not give up the powers belonging to the Legislative Yuan, and the comrades of the Legislative Yuan should also respect the powers belonging to the other branches. As for the powers of the Political Conference and the National Government, each branch should respect them even more, and should not come to violate our legislative spirit and Party governance system for the sake of something of a certain branch. Therefore, only by respecting each other can we be independently without harm. The designation of the public bond fund and the organization of the management committee are the powers of the Executive Yuan. The Central Government has issued public bonds more than once, and the precedents are all there, which cannot be erased. If we must cross the threshold of legislation and replace the Executive Yuan in cooking, and disrupt responsibilities, starting from the Central Government, it is by no means the original intention of the independence of the five powers. (2) The political system of our Party has a consistent spirit that cannot be obliterated. Violating this consistent spirit is tantamount to violating Party discipline. The Central Political Conference is the center of Party tutelage. The legislative procedure further clarifies the connection between the Central Political Conference and the Legislative Yuan. No matter which branch it is, it has no right to modify or resist and reject what has been decided by the Central Governance Conference. The amount of debt determined by the Central Political Conference for this disaster relief bond case is the same as the amount of debt originally determined by the Legislative Yuan, which is already consistent in general. If this kind of legal fact and comprehensive resolution cannot be understood, how is it different from having to tear up the legislative procedure and completely destroy the power of the highest political center? This is absolutely impossible. I think the comrades who clearly understand the Party's governance of the country and the political system of the National Government will definitely understand and will not misunderstand. (3) In addition to the mutual complement of the five powers and the consistent spirit, our Party has always had an important point left by history that can work together with one heart, that is, based on the collegial approach of mutual love and sincerity. Judging from the facts and the law, the National Government is now completely a collegial system. No matter which branch or department, it cannot force the government to agree to a proposal with the prejudice of one branch or one person and treat the National Government as a puppet. All important state affairs must be consulted first and then decided. Therefore, these decisions can be pleasant and harmonious and proceed smoothly. If the resolution of one branch must force other branches to be unable to, and even force the entire central government to be unable to, and even repeatedly delay the disaster relief bonds themselves, making the disaster victims wait to die, this is absolutely impossible. Moreover, the National Government Organization Law clearly stipulates that cases that cannot be resolved between branches should be decided by the National Government Conference. Therefore, the branches should respect the resolutions of the government. Based on the above points, I hope that the comrades of each branch will understand this point and dispel unnecessary misunderstandings. Therefore, I do not hesitate to speak frankly and make this report. The disaster victims who are waiting for relief while enduring death cannot wait for us to quibble and argue about right and wrong. The comrades of each branch should understand this difficulty and understand each other, hoping to achieve the goal of fighting together and completing the revolutionary responsibility. I am very fortunate.)

Dumping of Russian Goods Endangers Northern Manchuria 70

Total Imports of 22 Million in the First Half of the Year

State-Run Trading Branches Established in Various Border Areas

Harbin Correspondence: For months, the shops here have been panicked. The reason for the panic is the dumping of Russian goods, which has invaded Northern Manchuria and has become an overwhelming trend. The customs summaries of Suifenhe and Manzhouli before July 15 stated that the value of Russian goods imported in half a year was more than 22 million yuan. The staggering number has startled those who heard it. However, the border with Russia is thousands of miles long, such as Heihe, Tongjiang, Hulin, Mishan, and Dongning, Raodong, Suiyuan, and Luobei counties and towns, all have imports, but no one knows the value of them. Along the Eastern Railway, there are also mobile consumer cooperatives that sell goods by train, which has caused the Harbin merchants to feel extremely oppressed. All commercial markets have been destroyed as a result. Recently, Soviet Russia successfully purchased grain in the lower reaches of the Songhua River, and Harbin lost its economic center, and felt a greater threat. The merchants associations inside and outside the Daoli district have successively convened trade associations to study countermeasures. The only solution is to petition the government to restrict the import of Russian goods, but when the petition was submitted to the government, it was said that the Sino-Russian meeting was in the midst of negotiations, and it did not want to take decisive measures to cause disharmony between the two countries. However, there is no other good plan except to prohibit the import of Russian goods. The Special Police Management Office once agreed to collect a defense donation for Russian goods, and to add a 2.5% donation for every hundred yuan of value in addition to various regular taxes, in order to limit the smooth entry of Russian goods. After submitting the report to the Northeast Political Affairs Committee, it was rejected and instructed the Special Zone Administrative Chief Executive Office to discuss other laws. Until now, the Chief Executive Office has not yet replied. The so-called other law is actually difficult to imagine. A certain organization here recently reported to the Suifenhe police that Russia has recently established state-run commercial trading offices in various border areas, which will be the main agency for dumping goods to our border towns. Then Russia's sales plan will be carried out on a large scale, so the enlightened people in the business community recognize this as a very large crisis in Northern Manchuria. In two years, the trade of Northern Manchuria will be completely occupied by Russia. Recently, the two police offices in Te and Lu have respectively investigated the types and quantities of Russian goods exported and imported, and will report to the Chief Executive Office and submit it to the Central Government for approval to show the prevention policy. However, the Central Government has also heard of the dumping of Russian goods in Northern Manchuria for a long time, and has recently telegraphed the Chamber of Commerce to investigate and report, so as to decide on a plan. (3rd)

Five Counties' Disaster Victims Telegraph the Provincial Government to Order Mao and Li to Take Responsibility for Repairs 71

The Yancheng, Funing, Taixing, and Dongtai Disaster Relief Association stationed in the town telegraphed Chairman Ye, saying: To Jiangsu Provincial Government Chairman Ye Jun鑒, The collapse of the canal embankment is a catastrophe of immense proportions. The fault lies with the river affairs personnel, who failed to prepare in advance and fled completely afterward. Public opinion points to this, and there is no denying it. Previously, members of our association personally presented relief measures, which were entirely adopted by your government. You also expressed that if this is not handled well, you would have no face to face the central government again. This good news spread, and everyone was moved to tears. Later, we saw your personal inspection of the construction and the committee's repeated resolutions on various cases, all of which demonstrate sincerity. However, outsiders, unaware of the situation, have fabricated rumors about the penalty of dismissal and retention of Director Mao, claiming that the affected people are mostly dissatisfied. They do not know that the disaster was caused by him, and the lives and property of millions of people have been destroyed. Now, to have him reinstated to oversee repairs is only right. Unfortunately, the original plan did not include the words "responsible for repairs," so the river affairs personnel remain at large. In fact, confiscating the assets of these officials and assigning them to plug the breach would be enough. Now, we hear that these officials are trying every possible means to escape responsibility, as evidenced by Li Zhongqiang's undisguised joy at being ordered to be dismissed. We urge your government not to be misled by rumors and to order Mao Yisheng, Li Zhongqiang, and others to go to the construction site immediately and take responsibility for the repairs. This is the first request. Furthermore, your government has now hired Wang Shuxiang and others as members of the disaster relief committee. According to our association's telegraph of a few days ago, their role is only to guide. The responsibility for emergency repairs should still be borne by the original river affairs personnel. The original telegram can be reviewed. However, we hear that the Department of Construction intends to use this as an excuse to shirk responsibility. The breach-plugging project has not been actively carried out to date, which is disappointing to the people. Moreover, they are repeatedly blaming the flood on "the will of Heaven, which cannot be averted by human effort." Yesterday, we read in the newspaper that "Fifth Uncle" Tan and others discussed the aftermath of the project, stating that it would require at least ten million yuan and countless human sacrifices. Moreover, the land and sea are changing, and Shaobo Lake tends to shift eastward, which cannot be reversed by human effort. The decline of Shaobo Town is predetermined by Heaven. Although Chairman Ye will hire Wang, Wang's words are quite negative. After repeatedly reading this, our association feels that it is very unlike him. Your government's decision to hire Wang to join the disaster relief work must have been with Wang's prior agreement. Otherwise, why engage in empty gestures? As for the statement that the eastward shift of Shaohu is the will of Heaven and cannot be reversed by human effort, it sounds like the excuse of the Department of Construction and the current river affairs personnel to shirk responsibility. How could Wang, with his usual words and morals, echo them? Also, the breach-plugging project requires one hundred million yuan, a terrifyingly large sum, intended to keep the counties downstream submerged forever and to relieve the current river affairs personnel of their difficulties. Such a malicious psychology is surely not something Wang would say. There must be someone deliberately creating illusions and undermining the disaster relief plan. We urge your government to firmly carry out the original plan to save this great calamity. This is the second request. Furthermore, we were previously approved to distribute 100,000 yuan for emergency relief. Apart from the first distribution of over 30,000 yuan to various counties, when will the remaining 60,000 yuan be distributed? We urge your government to clarify this. This is the third request. The above-mentioned matters are of utmost importance. We earnestly request your immediate decision and a reply to comfort the people. We are immensely grateful. The Yancheng, Funing, Taixing, and Dongtai Disaster Relief Association stationed in the town respectfully presents this message.

Zhang Zhijiang's Reply to the Yancheng Reclamation Association Telegram 72

▲ There was no dispatch of troops to destroy the dykes of various companies. To the Joint Association of Yancheng Reclamation Companies in Northern Jiangsu: Your telegram has been read. The flood has caused disaster, and the people of several counties east of the canal are completely submerged, with deaths and displacement, which is deeply tragic. This office, mindful of the lives and property of the people, is doing everything within its power to rescue them. Every ordinary man and woman, every inch of land, is in our consideration. How could we destroy the salt farms without cause and disregard the lives of hundreds of thousands of tenant farmers? This time, the provincial government, in order to dredge the waterway to the sea in the Dongtai area, feared that the people on both sides might have misunderstandings and disputes, so it telegraphed this office to send a team to suppress them. This office, in order to maintain order, immediately sent a team. As for the dredging work, the provincial government has its own proper plans. If your association has any suggestions, you should directly submit them to the Jiangsu Provincial Government. Zhang Zhijiang (seal).

Moreover, in recent years, the tenant farmers have become increasingly assertive and easily incited. According to a telegram from the Xiaohai Tongsuo Company, there have already been casualties in the fighting between farmers and tenants. The number of tenant farmers in Dafeng is particularly large. The company's eastern area is high and the western area is low, which has long been understood. It can be calculated whether the removal of the dike can reduce the flow of water in the three counties. Otherwise, the sea defenses have been removed, the autumn floods are imminent, and the saltwater will flood inland, leaving the tenant farmers with no hope of survival. The harm will not be limited to the company. This matter concerns the lives of the people, and any negligence will lead to disaster. In addition to appealing to Director Zhang to assess the situation and not allow the disaster area to expand, we are sending this special telegram to your government for review. Please take immediate measures, investigate in detail, and handle the matter carefully. In the current situation, this association has a responsibility to speak out, and our conscience is concerned. We are deeply worried about the disaster caused by the械鬥械鬥, and we cannot but make this request. We are all trying to save those who are drowning, and there is no room for selfishness. We ask you to weigh the two harms and choose the lesser. Chairman, your knowledge and talent are admired throughout the world, and your mind is clear and unbiased. We sincerely submit this message. The Joint Association of Yancheng Reclamation Companies,

Investigation of the Disaster Situation in the Xinghua Area 73

Findings of the First Relief Team's On-Site Inspection

The First Relief Team of the Jiangbei Flood Relief Association set out from the province on the 30th of last month and returned to Zhenjiang at 9 a.m. on the 5th of this month, a journey of one week. The original purpose was to investigate the flood situation in the Xingdong area and distribute emergency relief. However, after arriving in Xinghua and distributing a small amount of the relief supplies, there was nothing left. Furthermore, with hundreds of refugees on board, it was impossible to go to Dongtai again. Therefore, after the work in Xinghua was completed, they returned to Zhenjiang. According to the report of Team Leader Liu, the disaster situation along the way and in the Xinghua area is as follows:

(1) The Flood Situation Along the Way: Comparing the disaster situation along the way, it can be divided into three sections. The first is between Xinghua and Yong'an, where the water is the highest and the disaster is the most severe. The water and sky are connected all the way, a vast expanse of water, covering countless acres. Traveling by boat, it is like entering Taihu Lake. Only the tops of trees are swaying on the surface of the water, and nothing else can be seen. People and livestock are drifting, and houses are destroyed, as if they have sunk to the bottom of the sea. Even the desperate cries for help from the refugees cannot be heard. Relief cannot be provided. Alas, Yong'an Town has suffered the most severely. Hundreds of lives in the entire town have been drowned. Only one family at the bridge entrance remains standing. The second is the area north of Qiaoshu, including Zhenwumiao, Yangjiazhuang, and Qiushuge. Although the disaster is more severe than before, the situation is very tragic. Some residents have built houses in the trees, while others are standing directly on the rooftops. Only cries for help can be heard. When the relief team travels, the residents, disregarding the danger, drive small boats and follow the waves to beg for relief. Some even come on a small plank or wooden basin. Men, women, old and young, are crowded together, kneeling and bowing, crying to the heavens, desperately seeking food. The scene is the most tragic I have ever seen. The people in the Zhenwumiao area are mostly sleeping on the embankments, without shelter from the wind and rain. The embankments are only level with the water surface, and any wind or rain would be very dangerous. Every time a relief team arrives, the refugees stand together begging for relief, with no less than a thousand people in each section. The relief supplies they carry are a drop in the bucket, not enough to solve the problem. They can only grit their teeth and speed away. The third is the area south of Qiaoshu, including Xiannv Town and Shaobo. The disaster is relatively light. The good fields have also become a vast expanse of water, but there is still land to be seen. Although some residents' houses have been washed away, half of them still have houses to live in and food to eat, which is incomparable to the areas above. The banks of Xiannv Town are several feet above the water, so there is no problem. Shaobo was in extreme danger during the flood. The main street also had three or four feet of water. The entire town is only three li long, but the embankments that were washed away, such as Liuzha, Sun Jimaozhou, Nantawangmiao, and Guanyi Qian Shimadou, number more than ten. The town's original rice market and Yangmujiang Lane in the north street were all washed away. About three hundred people were drowned, and about two thousand houses were damaged. Dilapidated houses and crumbling walls are everywhere, a desolate scene that is unbearable to witness. The water has now receded, and the entire town has escaped danger. Local people are working hard to reorganize. The embankments north of the town are also being repaired by the 25th Army, which has sent an engineering team. The disaster situation is even lighter south of Shaobo. The above sections are compared based on observations made along the road from Yangzhou to Xinghua. In short, when the water first flooded, the Gao and Shao areas bore the brunt and suffered the most severely. When the Che Nanxin Sanba opened and the breaches occurred on the east bank of the canal and north of Zhaoguan Dam, the water flowed directly downstream, pouring the water of Hongze, Gaoyou, and Shaobo Lakes, originating from the source, downstream. The low-lying areas of Yancheng, Funing, Xinghua, and Dongtai had no way to discharge and divert the water into the sea, so they had to become a泽国泽国. Therefore, in terms of the current water situation, the disaster in the Lixia River area is actually more severe than in the upper river areas. Relief measures should be taken urgently. According to those with water conservancy experience, in order to relieve the flood disaster in the lower river area, we should take advantage of the current slow water recession and rush to repair the breaches on the east bank of the canal and quickly find ways to excavate the Fan Gong Dike and dredge the Mao You River to lead the water into the sea. The lower river area may be saved. Otherwise, it may become a large lake, and it is impossible to know.

(2) The Current Situation in Xinghua: Xinghua is like the bottom of a pot, where all the waters converge, and it suffers the most severe disaster. Almost no place in the entire county is spared. According to local people, this flood is more than a foot deeper than the last one sixty-six years ago, when the Qing Shui Tan was flooded. Only a corner of the county government in the urban area is dry land. The rest has become a 泽国泽国. The lowest point is about four feet deep, and the highest point is also three feet deep. People travel by wading in the water, which reaches above the chest and abdomen. Their clothes are all wet. Some have specially built small boats about five feet long and three feet wide as transportation tools. Many houses are submerged in water and have collapsed. People mostly live in water pavilions. The water in the four villages is even higher, more than ten feet deep in the deepest places, and more than five or six feet deep in the shallow places. Wherever our (Liu's) relief boat went, within a radius of dozens of li, we did not see a single family cooking. Most of the villagers have no house to live in. Some have built wooden boards and straw mats into houses, some live in large temples and on opera stages, and some have built houses in the trees. Some are even buried in the water all day long. The state of panic is truly the most tragic in the world. When people die, there is no place to put them in the house, and there is no soil to bury them in the fields. Most coffins are hung on trees. The cattle have no grass to eat, and many have starved to death, so cheap that they are six or eight yuan each, and there are no buyers. Villagers mostly kill and eat them. Since Xinghua was surrounded by the flood, the riverbanks in the four villages are indistinguishable. The ferries have long been suspended, and there is no fixed schedule for the help boats. The telegraph poles have been washed down by the water, and the telegrams have not been connected for a long time. Transportation is blocked, and there is no communication. Outsiders are naturally full of doubts, and the truth is unknown. Even the people of Xinghua themselves say that they live in a land of despair, and that the county's rice and grain supply is only enough for ten days. All day long, people are in a panic. Since the arrival of our First Team and the first relief boat of the Relief Affairs Association on August 31, the people of Xinghua have begun to feel a little more at ease. County Magistrate Hua Zhen is ill and does not come out, and he rarely asks about the flood. Although local groups have a temporary organization for disaster relief, because the content is complex, there is little activity. It is hoped that in this time of great disaster, everyone will see righteousness and courage, cooperate to the end, and jointly rescue the crisis. It must be known that the disaster area is so vast and the refugees are so numerous that a few people cannot cope with it.

Inspection Report on the Gaoyou Disaster Area 74

Refugees on the West Canal Embankment Crying Bitterly for Their Families

Corpses Piled Up Like Mountains at Beiyaodun

Gaoyou correspondence: On the morning of the 3rd of this month at 7 a.m., I set out from Huayan Temple in the South Gate and headed north along the Canal Embankment to inspect the disaster area. Arriving at the southern end of Shuangrenjintou, I saw that the Canal Embankment there was cracked for more than four zhang. According to residents, the area was extremely dangerous around 12 p.m. on the 26th. When the northwest wind was blowing hard, huge waves directly washed against the embankment, causing it to collapse immediately. Emergency repairs were carried out, but to no effect. Two hours later, because the 25th Lipu south of the city and the Hehuatang, Xiaolubao, and Shaobo areas of Yangzhou also reported breaches, the water level in the Canal dropped by a foot, which saved the embankment. If the embankment had breached there, the whole city of Gaoyou would not have survived. From Shuangrenjintou to the Wangmiao section of the Canal Embankment, the population is dense, and vendors selling food are everywhere. The liveliness is unprecedented. There are more than twenty newly built straw sheds in the Pipa Lock, mostly housing refugees who live outside the North Gate. Their houses have been washed away by the water. There are many clothes piled up outside the sheds, soaked in water. The refugees are all disheveled and dirty, black and thin, and their condition is extremely pitiful. Going north, I arrived at Wangmiao, where there are many refugees. In addition to the house being full, there are many people sleeping in the courtyard. I met Zhao Huchen, the Inspector General of the Sixth District of the Water Police, who said that there were more than 5,000 refugees in the temple. From the 26th to the 28th, the refugees' food was supplied by his private funds. Now, the Gaobao You Patrol Team is receiving and maintaining relief from the Gaoyou Relief Branch. I then said goodbye and went north along the embankment. From the West Gate to Tonghu Bridge, there are more than a thousand straw sheds for refugees, with an estimated seven or eight thousand people. This area is entirely inhabited by residents outside the North Gate, and some refugees are crying in the sheds, because their family members were drowned in the water. The situation is extremely tragic. According to the refugees, the relief associations in the South Gate do not often come to this area to distribute relief, so there are many who are starving. From Tonghu Town to Qigongdian, the Canal Embankment is about a li long. The old and new dikes were destroyed by huge waves on the 25th and 26th. The stonework is completely exposed. The breach at Qigongdian is about twenty zhang long and about two zhang deep. The Qigongdian, which has stood for more than a thousand years, is no longer majestic on the top. There are many small boats parked below the breach. I hired a small boat to inspect back and forth in the southeast. The houses in Zuojiaxiang, Fangsheng Temple, and Tubakouhoujie have all been washed away. A vast expanse of water. About one thousand houses have been washed away in this area. From Tonghu Town, east of Zuojiaxiang, to the North City Gate and Tangzixiang, about two li long, eight out of ten houses have been washed away. Going north to the Royal Wharf, there is a small breach, about five zhang long and about two zhang deep.

The houses below the breach have also been washed away. Further north to Miaoxiangkou (i.e., Hehuatang), the breach there is larger, about sixty zhang long and about two zhang deep. The houses from Kongxinjie to the east of Dangjunlou below the breach have been completely washed away. A vast expanse of water. All that remains are the Yuheng Flour Mill and the Xingshang Gongji, but the houses have suffered heavy losses. When the boat arrived at Hehuatang, the waves were very large. I took the risk and ordered the boatman to cross. Arriving at Dangjunlou, the breach there is the largest of the four, about eighty zhang long and about two zhang deep. After the inspection, I returned to Zuojiaxiang by the same route, preparing to inspect the North Main Street. However, the road was blocked by the fallen houses and I could not go. I landed and walked back to the South Gate, arriving at 1 p.m. After lunch, I hired a boat from the Xiahe Haizi River to inspect north. From the boat, I could see a vast expanse of water in the east, south, and north. The city of Gaoyou is submerged in water, about ten zhang deep. When I arrived at the North and South Yaodun, there were about two thousand refugees gathered in the protective enclosure of the city. The four sides of the mound are surrounded by water. Refugees come and go by small boats. The Red Cross Society of this city has been sending people to salvage corpses in that area for several days, and the corpses are piled up on Beiyaodun, so the corpses are piled up like mountains on Beiyaodun. The situation is extremely tragic. The corpses have rotted and the stench is overflowing. Boats passing through the area cannot help but cover their noses. Crossing the East Gate, there are also a thousand refugees on the city wall, living in straw sheds. Passing through Haichao Temple, I saw that the temple and the houses were completely washed away. The boat can go directly to Taishan Temple. Half of the thirty-six houses in the front courtyard of the temple have collapsed. I entered through the back door. I was invited by the receptionist, Mr. Lian Kaixiang, to the office. According to him, there are a total of 1,860 refugees here. The previous day, some actors who performed at Qigongdian also lived here and set a fire, but fortunately it was extinguished and did not become a major disaster. I immediately sent someone to report to County Magistrate Wang, who then ordered the team to drive the actors out of the area. The order is now calm, but there is too little food. County Magistrate Wang sends eleven bags of foreign flour every day, which is less than four taels per person. Therefore, the refugees cannot eat their fill at every meal. Mr. Lian then led me to inspect the refugees' residences in Wenyoutai and Wanghulou for a week. I then bid farewell and left. I boarded the boat and went west to inspect the areas of Huashijie, Niuji, Yuetang, Chouhebian, Xixiangkou, Yingcheng, Xinqiao, and Zhuntian in the North Gate. The water depth varies from about four to five feet. Most of the families are empty. Some residents are living on the water pavilions. About seven out of ten houses along the way have been washed away by the water. The North Main Street from the North City Gate to the Model Bridge has now been drained of water. I landed and inspected along the way. The North Gate Bridge has been washed away by the water. The east side of the city gate has also been washed away at one corner. The houses on the North Main Street are still neat. Except for those that were washed away at the water's head, the rest are intact. However, Yuxingcheng Shoe Store, Cha Yongcheng Lime Store, and Wanshunchang Store, although they were not harmed by the flood, suddenly suffered a fire on the morning of the 27th of last month. All the houses were burned to the ground, which can be said to be a great misfortune. After the inspection, I returned to the South Gate on the same boat. It was already 7 p.m. (September 4)

Recent Defense Situation in Western Hunan 75

Chen Quzhen's Telegram

Rumors that the Guangdong-Guangxi Army is Sending Troops to Western Hunan

Beijing News: It was previously heard here that the Guangdong-Guangxi Army, in order to avoid the real and attack the empty, planned to sneak into western Hunan from the border of Guangxi and extend to the Yangtze River. The communications office of the newly compiled 34th Division stationed in Beijing telegraphed western Hunan to inquire. Now, we have received a reply telegram from Division Commander Chen, saying, "Your telegram is understood. I previously heard that the Guangdong-Guangxi Army was sending troops to western Hunan. I ordered Brother Wu Seng (Director of the Division's Office in the Provincial Capital) to investigate and report the news from the provincial capital. The story that the Guangdong-Guangxi Army is sending troops to western Hunan is unfounded. Moreover, our army's border defenses are solid. Even if evil rebels invade, we swear to meet them head-on with all our strength. If petty thieves cause trouble, we will also find ways to prevent and control them. Within the defense area of western Hunan, where we are responsible, security will be assured. Special reply, Chen Quzhen respectfully (seal). According to this, it can be known that western Hunan is as peaceful as usual. After receiving the telegram, Li Jimin, the director of the division stationed in Beijing, visited Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek to report on the defense situation in western Hunan. He was greatly gratified and promised to provide a large amount of military　equipment　to be transported to western Hunan through that office for replenishment. (September 7)

The Tragedy of the Guangdong Huizhou Ship Sinking 76

Capsized in the Shuilong River Due to Overloading

More Than One Hundred People Drowned, Only Dozens Rescued

Guangzhou correspondence: The Huizhou electric ship of the Xin Guangyuan Company, which travels between Guangzhou and Huizhou, has always been required to anchor at the ports along the way during its daily voyage, so that passengers can disembark and embark and load and unload cargo. The ship recently sailed from Huizhou to the province at 8 a.m. on August 30, with about 150 to 160 passengers and a large amount of cargo. After sailing, it normally passed through Boluo County and the Lulan area. It was noon when the ship arrived at Shilong City in Dongguan County. The Shilong Dike has always had a ferry pier for the provincial Huizhou ships. At that time, the Huizhou ferry docked as usual so that passengers could land. There were many passengers in Shilong that day. Before the ship approached the shore, the passengers were preparing to retrieve their luggage and crowded in one corner, causing the ship to lose its balance. When the ship was turning its rudder, the passengers were scrambling to disembark, causing the ship to suddenly tilt to one side. The side with the most weight went into the water first, and all the passengers on the side of the ship fell into the sea. Before long, seawater flowed into the ship, and in a flash, the entire ship sank. When it sank, unfortunately, the small windows next to the ship were completely closed, so none of the passengers in the cabin escaped. Those on the deck jumped into the water to seek help. For a time, the sound of crying shook the sky, and it was unbearable to hear. Neighboring ships, hearing the news, rushed to rescue them, but the river was turbulent, and rescue was difficult. Only thirty or forty people were rescued, and the rest were buried in the bellies of fish. After the ship sank, its bottom faced the sky and was swept by the current to the Longdi area under the railway bridge in Shilong. There were still hundreds of people trapped in the ship who could not escape. The Dongguan County branch office, hearing the news, immediately sent prosecutors to the scene to investigate and sent workers to salvage corpses on the riverbank. Within two days, only more than twenty bodies were salvaged on the surface of the water. In addition, the corpses trapped in the cabin have not yet surfaced. The shipping company has hired four boats and two barges and sailed to the scene of the accident to find ways to lift the sunken ship. The Convenient Hospital of this province has also prepared more than one hundred coffins to go and salvage the corpses. According to those who survived, about one hundred people were drowned in this accident, half of whom were women and children. It is said that the ship has never had so many passengers in the past. Recently, because the Qinsheng steamship, which also travels on the route, was damaged and entered the dock for repairs, only the Huizhou electric ship was traveling back and forth to the province, so the passengers suddenly became crowded, causing this tragic accident. (September 2)

Recent News on the Longhai Railway Project 77

The Lingtong Section Expected to Open Next Month

Since the resumption of construction on the Lingtong section of the western Longhai Railway this spring, there was an initial plan for completion in October. According to railway news, the section has seen rapid progress with no work stoppage. The roadbed from Lingshi to Tongguan is now fully completed, and tracks have been laid up to a certain point. Currently, passengers and small freight shipments heading west can travel on construction material trains to a certain village. It is expected that the Lingtong section will officially open to traffic on October 1st. After this section is opened, expansion towards Xi'an will continue to facilitate the implementation of the Northwest development plan. The Railway Administration issued the following announcement yesterday: (It has been determined that track laying on the Lingtong section of this railway has reached a certain village. During this construction period, to facilitate merchants and the public, passenger and small freight shipments will be carried on material trains starting August 26th. This has been reported and circulated, so it is hereby announced.)

The Longhai Railway Bureau received an order from the Ministry of Railways to include the railway as a key east-west line in North China in a joint immigration transportation scheme involving the Beining, PingSui, Jinpu, and PingHan railways. Starting September 1st, joint tickets will be issued. The railway has designated five stations: Shangqiu, Kaifeng, Luoyang, Shanzhou, and Zhengzhou, with Zhengzhou as the final destination. Each ticket will be discounted by 40% of the third-class fare, costing one yuan and forty cents from Shangqiu to Zhengzhou, five jiao from Bian (Kaifeng) to Zhengzhou, eight jiao and five fen from Luo (Luoyang) to Zhengzhou, and one yuan eight jiao and five fen from Shan (Shanzhou) to Zhengzhou. These joint tickets are limited to those heading to the Northeast and Northwest to open up land. A certificate from an immigration agency or proof from the county government is required when purchasing tickets. When transferring to trains heading north from Zhengzhou, new tickets must be purchased. The fares from Zhengzhou to Fengtai are six yuan, from Fengtai to Tianjin are seven jiao, and from Tianjin to Shenyang or Yingkou are four yuan each. Regulations also specify the tonnage of luggage and farm tools immigrants can transport together.

Liu Guitang's Troops Flee to Feicheng 78

Ma Hongkui Has Dispatched Troops to Encircle and Suppress

A dispatch from Jinan reports that Liu Guitang's bandit troops suddenly fled north from Liangshan, stopping in the western part of Feicheng. The local militia clashed with them once, suffering significant losses. According to official sources, Liu Guitang's troops were still entrenched in the Yemazhuang area west of Feicheng as of yesterday (the 5th). In addition to pursuing troops following in pursuit, Ma Hongkui, based on repeated urgent telegrams from officials and civilians in Feicheng and a delegation to Tai'an requesting a swift deployment of troops to intercept them and prevent further flight, reportedly dispatched over a thousand men to Feicheng. They are currently deploying defenses and are twenty to thirty li away from Liu Guitang's bandit troops, but there has been no contact yet.

When Liu Guitang's troops passed through the South Gate of Jining, they looted the area, causing enormous losses to the business community of Jining. The Department of Civil Affairs dispatched personnel to Jining today to investigate. The General Headquarters, concerned about the rampant banditry in western Shandong, has specially dispatched Ning Chunxiao, commander of the 64th Brigade, with a regiment of troops from Yanzhou to Jining to provide deterrence. Tang Yaoxun's 65th Brigade has also dispatched a regiment of troops from Jinan to Juancheng on foot, to join forces with Gu Liangyou's command of the Shandong Militia to exterminate the bandits, stabilize western Shandong, and maintain security.

People coming from the city say that Liu Guitang's troops have fled into Feicheng territory, occupying the Xiaogangshan and Anling Station areas, burning, looting, and doing whatever they please. Unable to resist, the villagers have no choice but to flee together, and the sound of weeping along the way is harrowing. Those who are slower to flee have to submit to their abuses. It is also heard that Liu's bandits, unhappy with the villagers' hospitality, set fire to more than twenty village houses. Since before yesterday (the 4th), many of these bandits have also been seen in the Yemazhuang and Tuntou villages. It is heard that Ma Hongkui, General Commander of the 15th Route Army, in response to the people's

Page 11

Important News

request, has sent a regiment of Ma Quanliang's Brigade stationed at Dawenkou to Feicheng to suppress the bandits. They arrived in Feicheng territory yesterday (the 5th) and are expected to issue orders to encircle and suppress the bandits today (the 6th) or tomorrow (the 7th). After receiving a telegram from Feicheng, Governor Han Fuju also instructed the Third Route Army to deploy a unit to Feicheng to assist in the suppression before he left for Henan, so as to eliminate the bandit scourge as soon as possible. The Feicheng County government, as various units of troops are about to arrive in the county, and to understand the inside story of the bandit situation, also sent personnel to the bandit area yesterday (the 5th) to investigate, in order to exterminate the bandits (6th).

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 79

Second Group of Patrol Officers Sent to Province for Training. The Department of Civil Affairs has established a police officer training school and issued an order to the Public Security Bureaus of various counties to select current patrol officers for training in the province. This county previously dispatched three patrol officers, including Luo Zhenglin from the Second District, to study, and they have now graduated and returned to Songjiang, resuming their original positions. Now, having received orders to send a second group to the province for training, Director Shen has designated Zong Yulin from the Eighth Substation, Jiang Shengwu from the Ninth Substation, and Chen Shuliang from the Tenth Substation to carry their credentials and proceed to the province on the 10th. To fill the vacancies, Xu Xuejiang, Meng Zhaoying, and Qian Haiquan, police academy graduates assigned to this county awaiting assignment, will be appointed to act as substitutes.

Danger Arises Again in the Second Section of the Seawall. Sections 3 and 4 of the seawall at Jinshanwei in this county were severely damaged by the violent winds and waves last month, and over a thousand wooden piles were uprooted, leaving the people of coastal counties in imminent danger. The County Chamber of Commerce here urgently telegraphed the provincial government to appeal, and received a reply today (We have instructed the Department of Construction to send personnel to supervise the urgent reinforcement of the seawall. We hereby reply.) Unexpectedly, the First Section of the dike is also in danger due to the wind and rain two days ago (the 6th) and the excessive high tide. Patrolman Li Yihua, seeing the tense situation, urgently sent a letter to District Chief Xu to discuss emergency rescue measures at Jinshanwei. However, Songcheng is lower than sea level, resembling the bottom of a cauldron. Now that the autumn high tide is approaching, it is hard to imagine the disastrous consequences if precautionary measures are not taken. Although the local authorities have sent personnel to investigate, the people are eagerly awaiting the responsible officials to formulate practical and safe measures to protect the lives of several counties.

The Third Security Battalion Captures a Notorious Bandit. Yu Guihe, a notorious bandit operating in eastern Pinghu, is a member of Taibao A Shu's gang. He specializes in committing crimes in the eastern countryside. He was apprehended by Fang, battalion commander of the Third Security Battalion, while loitering in Beicang Town two days ago after his whereabouts were discovered. Calamity Never Comes Alone. Zha Genggeng, a native of Changshu, had his brick and tile boat sunk by a coal boat under the Darihui Bridge in Suzhou city on the 1st of this month, drowning Zha Genggeng's wife and daughter. Subsequently, Zha Genggeng's clansman Zha Hehe went to Changshu to inform Zha Genggeng's relatives and then brought seven relatives, including Zha A Er, to Suzhou to handle the aftermath. However, on the way to Suzhou, their boat encountered a bandit ship in Yezhangjing, and all the cash they were carrying was looted, leaving them penniless upon arrival in Suzhou, a truly miserable situation. The shops outside Xumen then pooled together fifty-five yuan to hire workers to salvage the sunken brick and tile boat. Unfortunately, just as they were raising the boat, a stone barge came along, riding the wind and waves, and smashed the brick and tile boat that was about to be salvaged into two pieces. The owner of the stone boat, Guo Qinglang, was immediately taken to the local substation and transferred to the Public Security Bureau for questioning.

A Xiamen Native Commits Suicide in an Inn. Unexpectedly, on the afternoon of the 6th, he secretly swallowed six bottles of tranquilizer pills. By 8 PM that night, the tea attendant discovered that he had died. The responsible police district reported the incident to the local court, which dispatched personnel yesterday (the 7th) to examine the body. Qian Yuming was wearing a Western suit and appeared to be a student. The reason for his suicide is unknown.

Autumn Cocoons Soon to Be Weighed and Sold. The early batch of autumn silkworms in Wuxi has already spun their cocoons. The Cocoon Industry Association held a general meeting of members at its clubhouse in Xujialong, in the city yesterday at 3 PM. More than one hundred members, including Yuan Fuchen and Chen Yuanzhu, attended. Hua Shaochun, the chairman, reported on the silk price situation and the autumn silkworm situation this year. The prospects are not very good. Each business opening to buy cocoons must pay a deposit of fifty yuan. The members discussed the price of autumn cocoons and decided on a price of sixty yuan per dan. Weighing and selling will begin once the cocoons are available, and the rest will be handled as in previous years. The meeting adjourned after the discussion. Also, in the fifth district of the county (i.e., Tianshang City), the autumn silkworms in the Yanqiao Village, Qianchang Bridge, Zhangcun, Sitou, and Xizhang Xiaolishi areas are generally safe. However, the cold weather a few days ago caused the discovery of white silkworms, but the losses are not significant. The early batch of "three gourd" variety has already spun its cocoons, and the silkworms are still healthy. Cocoon businesses in Chang'an, Qiaotai, and Pingqiao areas have already started buying cocoons at a high price of sixty yuan, but there are few sellers. The early harvest is less than 10%. The later batch can also spin cocoons in another one or two days. This autumn silkworm crop is almost half a month later than usual. Mulberry leaves have decreased significantly due to being submerged in water, which has had a significant impact. Therefore, leaf prices are incredibly high, selling for three yuan and five jiao to four yuan per dan, but there is still nowhere to buy them.

The New Public Security Bureau Director Expected to Take Office. Xu Jigui, the Director of the Public Security Bureau of this county, has been mediocre in his administration since taking office. He has recently been ordered to transfer to Qingpu. His replacement, Hua Pu (Jianren), a native of this county, appointed by the provincial committee, is scheduled to arrive in Wuxi on the 13th of this month to take over.

Gao, recalling the difficult life, jumped into the river on the evening of the 3rd in an attempt to end his life. Fortunately, neighbors rescued him, and he was able to live again.

Anqing 89

Guangfeng and Guangji Dikes Desperately Awaiting Relief. The Guangfeng Dike in Dongliu County is located on the opposite bank of Anqing, with over ten mu of fields and a population of over ten million. The rural economy has been difficult due to years of disaster and crop failure. Since the beginning of summer this year, there have been continuous heavy rains, and the river tides have been surging. On a recent windy and rainy night, it suddenly collapsed. The surrounding hundreds of miles have become a vast expanse of water, with people and livestock drifting and houses destroyed, a very tragic situation. In addition, the Guangji Dike outside the East Gate of Anqing spans Tongcheng and Huaining counties, with seven to eight million mu of fields and over two million people. It produces several million shi of grain each year and is one of the largest dikes in Anhui. It also collapsed the other day, and many people and livestock were drifting. Now, the general refugees, due to the cool breeze, have no clothing or food, and their situation is precarious. Therefore, the Guangfeng and Guangji dikes deeply hope that all sectors will quickly provide relief to save the survivors.

Special Article

Afforestation Is the Only Way to Save Us From Floods - Meng Shu 90

This flood in China has spread throughout the country and is unprecedented. The loss of life and property amounts to many trillions, and China, from the government to the common people, is at a loss and can only sigh helplessly. It is pitiful that the general public is disturbed by both internal warfare and the harm of floods. The government is using all its strength to suppress bandits and eliminate communists, which is admirable. I also hope that the government will use all its strength to fight the floods. Who says human power cannot overcome nature?

Everyone knows that it rains too much, but why does a lot of rain in China always cause great harm? Other countries, such as Japan, also have a lot of rain, but why doesn't it cause disasters? Is it that God is kind to others but unkind to us? There must be a reason for it. What is the reason? It is whether or not there is attention to forests.

China not only has no forests, but even if there are any, the trees are cut down before they are fully grown. One aspect is the arbitrary destruction by the people, and the second is that the government does not protect the existing forests. This has been going on for thousands of years, so China has become the world's leading country in lacking forests. The mountains are bare for thousands of miles, not a single tree can be seen. As the years pass, the geology deteriorates, and the general public is still not awakened from their dreams.

Why does a lot of rain in China cause great harm? For example, if a hillside has all the trees cut down, when summer comes and it rains heavily, the rainwater falls from above with a kind of gravity. As the years pass, the surface of the hillside has been hardened by raindrops and cannot store water. Therefore, all the rainwater flows down the hillside, and at the same time, stones, soil, fine sand, etc., are also washed down by the hillside water. Therefore, the speed of the water flow increases, becoming what is called a kind of terrible torrent. Why is it terrible? Because (1) it can not only destroy embankments, but also destroy our cultivated farmland and our houses, (2) it can make the riverbed higher, which is quite dangerous for navigation, (3) it makes fertile arable land in the plains covered with sand and stones, turning it into barren land.

In other words, without forests, the ground cannot store water, and all the rainfall turns into torrents that flow into the rivers. The rivers cannot eliminate the sudden influx of water from various places in a short period of time, and if heavy rain continues to fall, the water level will rise, and floods will occur. Once floods occur, farmland is destroyed, and people have no food, leading to famine. If there is a famine after a flood, this is an unchanging truth throughout the ages. If we understand this, we will know the origin of floods in our country.

Now let's talk about why Japan (and the European and American powers as well) has a lot of rain but doesn't have disasters. This is the result of their attention to forests. Now I will describe the details, taking the above as an example. If we were to afforest this empty hillside, and assuming that this hillside has become a forest, what would happen when it rains heavily in the summer? Of course, the flood damage could be reduced. If the forests across the country are well managed, the flood damage could be completely eliminated. Why?

(1) Because the branches and leaves of broad-leaved forests can absorb one-third of the water, and the branches and leaves of forests with coniferous trees (most common in Japan) can absorb one-half of the water. Afterwards, the rainwater absorbed by these branches and leaves evaporates into the air. As for the excess rainwater that the branches and leaves cannot absorb, it flows into the ground.

(2) Before talking about the water flowing into the ground, we should talk about the geology under the forest. Because we have forests, and the leaves and branches that fall on the ground every winter gradually dry out. The same happens in the third year. Thus, every winter, the fallen leaves accumulate on the ground, so the ground surface has a thick layer of leaves. This layer of leaves has two effects: first, the lower layer of leaves decomposes and mixes with the soil, forming black soil, which can be used as fertilizer and also makes the land fertile, providing nutrition for the trees; second, this layer of leaves has a kind of sponge-like quality for rainwater, able to hold a large amount of water, and absorbing water five, six, or even nine times its own weight. Therefore, a lot of the water flowing into the ground is absorbed by the layer of leaves.

(3) When the layer of leaves reaches saturation, a portion of the water is evaporated by sunlight, and the rest flows into the ground in droplets, becoming spring water.

(4) As for the smallest amount of water that cannot be contained, it flows elsewhere. But in the paths it passes, it encounters endless obstacles: if it doesn't encounter tree trunks and branches, it encounters mosses and other herbaceous plants; if it doesn't encounter tree roots underground, it encounters leaf layers, etc. These obstacles have the function of a funnel. They can make the water flow slowly and can separate the stones and sand from the water. Finally, the smallest amount of water that cannot be contained flows into the river at the slowest speed. Therefore, the riverbed does not rise, and the river water does not rise. Sometimes it rises slightly, but it doesn't do any harm.

In other words, if we pay attention to forests, not only can forests be used to remove most of the rainwater, but they can also turn a large amount of rainwater into slow-moving water. Even if heavy rain continues to fall, the river water can flow away calmly. Farmland can be irrigated, and people have enough food and clothing. Therefore, the wealth and civilization of a country, and the attention to forests, is a most important element.

Another thing that can cause floods is snowmelt. Snow accumulates in the mountains and does not melt in winter. If there are no forests, hot rain or sunlight in the spring and summer will completely touch the snow, so it melts faster, and there is a risk of flooding. If there are forests, their branches, etc., can block the complete contact with rain or sunlight. The snow melts slower, and floods are less likely to occur.

From the above, the relationship between forests and floods is very important. European and American countries have always had relatively developed forests. The governments are also continuously promoting afforestation. One reason is that European and American industries are developed and require too much timber. The second is that sometimes there are still small floods, so they constantly encourage afforestation. The attention that European and American countries pay to the lives of their people can be seen from this. However, afforestation is not something that can be achieved overnight. The ancients said, "The plan for ten years lies in planting trees." I alone think that this is not enough. If the government wants to engage in afforestation, now is the time. Otherwise, such floods will continue to emerge, and the national pulse is in danger. (Sent from Nancy, France)

Recovering Education Rights in Concessions 91

The Municipal Education Bureau Requests Contributions from Various Concessions

Twelve Percent for Education Funding is Underway

(China Eastern News Agency) Regarding the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau's recovery of education rights in concessions, yesterday, according to Lu Buqing, section chief of the Second Section of the Municipal Education Bureau, speaking to a reporter from the China Eastern News Agency, it is not appropriate to say that the education rights within the concessions of this port have not been lost and recovered. Annual Anniversary of the Association of Belgian Alumni 93

The day before yesterday (the 6th), at 2:00 PM, the General Association of Chinese Students Who Studied in Belgium held its first anniversary meeting at the Yipinxian Grand Auditorium on Xizang Road. Approximately forty members attended. Li Yingbiao, representing Belgium, presided, and Yang Qi served as the recorder. First, the chairman reported on the work of the past year, followed by a discussion on amending the constitution and re-electing officers. Li Yingbiao, Yang Qi, Jiang Wenxin, He Shangping, Chen Qifu, and five others were elected as executive committee members. Liao Songxue, Yang Sifu, and Liu Zhimou were elected as supervisory committee members. The meeting adjourned at 5:30 PM, followed by a dinner. In addition to all members and their families, invited guests included Fan Zhengbo, Nong Ruhui, and foreign guests such as the Belgian Vice-Consul He Mengshi. At the dinner, Wang Jingqi first gave a speech, saying that what he hopes from the Belgian alumni is not only that they will make full use of the skills and knowledge they acquired during their studies to contribute to China, but also, and most importantly, that they will not forget the Belgian national spirit and perseverance—the ability to be peaceful and to strive—and take it as our model. If two or three Chinese people insist that small and weak countries cannot have fair diplomacy, cannot have prosperous industries, and cannot have the ability to resist powerful neighbors, the alumni will certainly not believe them, because the example of Belgium is there to prove that things are accomplished by human effort. Then, the Belgian Vice-Consul, He Shangping, Li Yingbiao, and others delivered speeches one after another, and lottery tickets were prepared to help with the fun. The first prize was a gramophone, won by Wang Jingqi, who then donated it back to the association. The gathering ended happily at 10:00 PM.

Telecommunications School Recruits Wired Radio Students 95

Oral Examination, Physical Examination, and Written Examination Have All Been Completed

To Be Submitted to the Ministry for Approval in the Coming Days, Classes Start in Early October

The Telecommunications School of the Ministry of Transportation recruited forty new students for the elementary wired radio class this year. A total of 342 people applied. On the 5th, the following were held at the school: (1) Oral examination, with three items: geography, English, and attitude; (2) Physical examination, with four items: hearing, vision, wrist, and diseases. A total of 325 candidates took the exam, and 17 were absent. It was completed at 5:00 PM that afternoon. On the 6th, the written examination was held at the junior high school of Shanghai High School, divided into two sessions. The first session started at 8:30 AM, and the papers were distributed. From 9:00 AM to 12:00 PM, the subjects were Party Principles, Chinese Language, and English. The second session started at 1:30 PM, and the papers were distributed. From 2:00 PM to 5:00 PM, the subjects were Mathematics, Physics and Chemistry, and Geography. A total of six subjects were tested throughout the day, with one hour for each subject. A total of 317 candidates completed the exam. The supervisors sent by the ministry and all the faculty and staff of the school were present to supervise the exam, and the order was very good. All the test papers were marked with secret codes and have been sent to the faculty members of each subject for evaluation and grading. The results will be submitted to the ministry for review and approval in the next few days and are expected to be announced this month. Classes will start in early October.

7:30 PM in the Basketball Hall

The disaster relief basketball game organized by the Physical Education Association will be held for three consecutive days starting tonight. Last Night's Basketball Game: Qingguang Wins Big Over Military Academy 101

Result: 29 to 17

Tomorrow Night's Confrontation with Jinan

The Nanjing Central Military Academy basketball team made its debut the night before last, defeating the Artillery Team by two points. Last night, at 7:30 PM, they competed with Qingguang, and as a result, lost 17 to 29. Tomorrow night at 7:30 PM, they will confront Jinan.

▲ The Military Academy is a Flash in the Pan: The military academy players are tall and strong. At the start of the game, they made a surprising move. Li Gongyu and Huang Guangqian successively scored points, earning as many as four points and creating a powerful momentum, making people shudder. However, the Qingguang veterans have been through many battles, and victory or defeat is not enough to move their hearts. Once the enemy's situation is detected, defeating the enemy is as easy as turning one's hand. Starting with Tan Dahua's three-pointer, Xu Kepei and others continued to advance fiercely, completing fourteen points in one breath. Although the military academy was brave, there was no room for counterattack. In the first half, Qingguang had fourteen points, and the military academy had four points.

▲ Qingguang Showed Mercy: Starting in the second half, Zhang Jinxiang scored in the basket, and Xu Kepei followed suit. With Qingguang's victory already determined, they took turns sending generals to respond. At this time, the military academy took the opportunity to attack and made some improvements. The short general Yin Hanchu's movements were interesting and his skills were also quite impressive. As a result of the game, Qingguang won by a large margin of twenty-nine to seventeen over the military academy. The referee was Shao Ji.

Race Meeting Preparatory Performance 103

Yesterday (6th) at 4 pm, the Chinese Race Walking Association specially selected new talents at the China Athletics Field to prepare to join the City Games performance race walking. Unexpectedly, it rained heavily all day, and the postponement was imminent. Fortunately, after 3 o'clock, the sky suddenly cleared, and the contestants began to report one after another. When the clock struck four times, Mr. Lu Yutian grouped and called the roll, and then Mr. Zhang Zaocai gave the order. Messrs. Shi Youhui, Shi Jinsheng, and Yao Wenhui timed the race, and Zhou Yuyu, Le Meigang, Zhang Zao, Jiu Hoge, Ren Cai Shuyan, and Lu Yutian supervised. In addition, the Boy Scouts of the 270th Regiment were on the scene to provide first aid and maintain order. Therefore, as a result, many people completed the 5,000-meter run with excellent results within 27 or 28 minutes. It can be seen that in the future, maintaining the International Race Walking Championship can be predicted. The list of players joining the City Games performance competition will be submitted to the Municipal Education Bureau in the coming days. Furthermore, in view of the fact that those who are old, such as Ge Zhonggao, and those who are young, such as Wang Mengmao, have achieved considerable results, they are also included for promotion and encouragement.

Liu Jian Discusses with Lin Baohua the Deliberation of the Top Ten Chinese Tennis Rankings 104

Lin Baohua, a Chinese tennis master who has been away for a long time and returned to Shanghai, published an article on the "Top Ten Chinese Tennis Players" in the Times on September 4. The order listed is quite flawed. Although his words are not official, the impact on the facts is very significant. Because this kind of statement lacks a factual proof, and the ten outstanding figures he mentioned are all written from love and hatred, in order to give the people of the country a real understanding, I do not hesitate to venture to state as follows:

(1) The Narrowness of the Location: The ten outstanding figures discussed by Mr. Lin are limited to Beijing, Tianjin, Shanghai, and Singapore. How can the two words "nationwide" be included? Moreover, South China has always produced talents, and there are many well-known figures in the tennis world today. How can they be allowed to be neglected?

(2) Lack of Facts: Mr. Lin indirectly occupies the first seat, degrading others, which gives people a kind of aversion. Moreover, it is difficult to determine the good guys sitting in the top three chairs without going through a kind of real competition. If you rely solely on the victory over Qiu in the past to put yourself in the first seat, place Qiu Feihai in the middle, and demote Lin Wangsu to the back, the injustice is obvious. Recalling the battle between the two Lins (Lin Baohua and Lin Wangsu played against each other before Lin Baohua fought against Qiu Feihai. Lin Wangsu won two sets in a row and took the lead. It was not finished due to darkness. Later, Lin Baohua did not finish the game for other reasons.) Lin Wangsu had a great chance of defeating Lin Baohua. If Qiu and Lin (Wangsu) are compared, then Lin is far inferior to Qiu (In various competitions in Singapore over the years, Lin Wangsu only won against Qiu Feihai once, and lost repeatedly in the rest of the battles.) Therefore, the order of the top three is currently a major suspense. As for the rest, such as:

Gao Huimin: Although Gao is the master of Beijing, his skills are mediocre and he has no special strengths. When Gao once represented North China in the national zonal competition, he made a debut in Shanghai, but was defeated by the generals of East China. It seems that there is no basis for Lin to place him in the fourth seat. And there are many people in the country who are better than Gao's skills, such as Luo Wenhui and Wu Renguang in Hong Kong, Gao Chixun in Guangzhou, and Cai Chunliang (transliteration) and Lin Yuehan in Singapore.

Gao is really no match.

Zheng Zhaojia: Zheng is a promising new player, young and handsome, with unlimited prospects. Unfortunately, he suffered from stomach problems this year and rarely practiced. However, judging from his level and hitting method, he is still in his infancy. It is not yet time to include him in the list of ten outstanding figures. According to the national games last year, Zheng represented Shanghai in Hangzhou and was defeated by the Zhejiang player Chen Naixin in the preliminary round. Checking his past achievements, in addition to winning the student singles championship in Tianjin and winning the Chinese Open doubles championship with Lin Baohua last year, he has no other significant achievements. Lin said that he had defeated Jiang Daozhang, which is a mistake and should be corrected.

Jiang Daozhang: Mr. Jiang has a large physique, so he feels a little slow when moving. Although his skills have not reached the point of perfection, he is now making progress day by day. How can it be said that his golden age is over? This can be proved by Jiang's battles against Can's Leed and Day's Machida in the Rotary Cup. How can Lin, who relegated him under Gao and Zheng, not complain?

The rest, such as Wu Shaoxiang and Liang Baokui, are all rising stars, but there are people everywhere in the country whose skills are equal to theirs. If they are included in the first-class masters, it is a theory of likes and dislikes. Although I am in my thirties, I have always loved tennis. Although my skills are not good, I have accumulated more than ten years of experience and have deep friendships with masters from all over the world. I think I have a silly idea, so I dare to discuss the order of the ten outstanding figures discussed by Mr. Lin in order to match the facts, and not to slander Mr. Lin. Here is the list of the ten outstanding figures I have cited. I don't know whether the tennis community agrees with it or not. I still ask for advice.

(1) Lin Baohua (order undecided)

(2) Qiu Feihai (order undecided)

(3) Lin Wangsu (order undecided)

(4) Cai Chunliang (Chua Choon Leong): Note that when Qiu Feihai won the Malayan Islands Championship in Singapore for three consecutive years, Cai was repeatedly the runner-up, and in 1925 he defeated the first master of the Philippines, Aligan, in the Philippines.

(5) Luo Wenhui: Hong Kong Open Singles Champion last year

(6) Jiang Daozhang

(7) Wu Shigang

(8) Lin Yuehan

(9) Ma Chixun: Singles and Doubles Champion of the National Games in Hangzhou in the 19th year

(10) Gao Huimin or He Jialiu
