Local News

Jiangsu Provincial Government Pledges Loans to Banking Sector 110

Results of Consultation: Intent to Approve

Hu Puan, Director of the Civil Affairs Department of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, Xu Baoying, Director of the Finance Department, Wang Yiting, Chairman of the Jiangsu Flood Relief Association, and Cheng Jingsheng, a member of the association, hosted a banquet for the banking sector at the Bankers' Association yesterday afternoon. Many people including Lin Kanghou attended. Chairman Wang Yiting reported on the disaster situation in northern Jiangsu. In addition to the fact that more than 12,000 people have been sheltered and more than 40,000 people have been transported out of the disaster area, they also consulted with the Jiangsu Provincial Government on mortgaging 2.5 million in construction bonds to the banking sector for cash. As a result of the consultation, it is heard that the banking sector has agreed to approve the loan and will hold a meeting today to discuss it. It is estimated that the bonds can be mortgaged at a 60% discount, with cash of 1.5 million yuan. It is proposed to hand over 60,000 yuan to the Jiangsu Flood Relief Association for disaster relief and 90,000 yuan to the Canal Engineering Aftermath Committee to handle the blockage of the breach in the Canal.

Disaster Relief Updates from Various Provinces - Yesterday's News 111

News from the Flood Relief Committee

▲ The National Government Flood Relief Committee held its second regular meeting yesterday. Previously, a first standing committee meeting was held regarding the purchase of American wheat for disaster relief. However, due to the chairman, Mr. Song Ziwen, going to Beijing, meetings had not continued. Now, it is known that Mr. Song arrived in Shanghai from Beijing the day before yesterday. In addition to holding discussions with Mr. Zhu Ziqiao, a standing committee member, at the Ministry of Finance's Shanghai office at 10:00 AM and 12:00 PM yesterday regarding the American wheat issue, he also convened a second regular meeting at 5:30 PM yesterday at his residence on Rue Pichon in the French Concession. Attendees included Chairman Song Ziwen, standing committee members Zhu Ziqiao, Xu Shiying, and Kong Xiangxi (Liu Shangqing was absent). Foreign committee members Baker and Younger were also present as observers. The discussion lasted for a considerable time. According to Secretary Zeng Rongpu, the results cannot be disclosed yet. However, according to Standing Committee member Xu Shiying, there were detailed discussions on issues such as American wheat and disaster relief bonds. Furthermore, the four methods proposed by Xiong Xiling of the Red Swastika Society for raising large sums of money were also brought up by Committee Member Zhu for informal exploration.

▲ National Committee Meeting to be Held Tomorrow: Song Ziwen, Chairman of the National Government Flood Relief Committee, announced that the National Flood Relief Committee meeting is scheduled to be held at 3:00 PM on Wednesday, September 9th, at the Central Bank Building.

▲ Liaison Group Held Meeting Yesterday: The Liaison Group of the Flood Relief Committee held its first committee meeting at 10:00 AM yesterday at the group's office at the Industrial and Commercial Visiting Bureau, No. 4 Hankou Road. After formalities, Chairman Kong Ren first reported on the establishment of the group, followed by discussion and resolution of the following cases: (1) Reorganization of the group. Resolved to change from five sections to four, with the publicity section merged into the general affairs section. (2) Recommendation to the general assembly regarding the appointment of committee members from all sectors to serve on various groups. Resolved: passed. (3) Recommendation to the general assembly to stop transporting disaster victims to Shanghai. Resolved: passed. (4) The Japanese China Flood Relief Association entrusted the "Amagi Maru" to transport 20,000 bags of rice, 60,000 bags of flour, 30,000 woolen blankets, and 10,000 cans of milk, scheduled to arrive in China in mid-September for disaster relief. The committee should send personnel to liaise. Resolved: Director Guo is responsible for handling this matter. (5) Lu Gan Chen reported that the YMCA had telegraphed the Geneva and New York headquarters to notify charitable organizations around the world to donate for disaster relief and that there was a youth cooperation plan. Resolved: Actively liaise. (6) Zeng Rongfu reported that the American Salvation Army will come to China to establish soup kitchens. Resolved: Welcome. The meeting adjourned at 12:15 PM. A second meeting will be called by the chairman at a later date.

Zhu Qinglan Narrates the Tragic Situation of Floods in Various Provinces 112

Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, the Shanghai Special City Party Headquarters held the weekly memorial service for Dr. Sun Yat-sen and invited Mr. Zhu Qinglan to speak about the tragic situation of floods in various provinces in the Southeast to expand publicity. The meeting was presided over by Mr. Pan Gongzhan, a standing committee member of the City Party Headquarters. After the ritual, a brief report on last week's work was given, followed by an introduction of Mr. Zhu Qinglan to deliver his speech. The following is the speech by Mr. Zhu: (Ladies and Gentlemen, I am both happy and worried to meet you all today. I am happy that I have the opportunity to speak today, but I am worried about the floods in various provinces and cities across the country, where the disaster situation is very serious. I am happy that Shanghai is spared and has a piece of clean land, but I am worried about whether the people across the country will pay attention to this flood and give the best possible help. This spring, I personally went to Shaanxi to inspect the severe disaster situation there. The severity and complexity of the disaster was rarely seen in history. In March, I came to Shanghai to invite leaders from all walks of life in Shanghai to discuss fundraising. I am grateful to the groups and philanthropists in this city for their enthusiastic donations, raising 400,000 gold coins to take to Shaanxi for disaster relief. I dare not boast about the results, but the desolate and barren land of the past is now filled with the sounds of chickens and dogs, and men and women are farming in the fields. Although the local vitality has not been fully restored, the people's livelihood has begun to show a glimmer of hope. This is something to be gratified by the people of this city. On behalf of the hundreds of thousands of disaster victims in Shaanxi, I bow deeply in gratitude. This year, the disaster situation in Gansu is also very serious, coupled with war and traffic obstruction. I went to inspect despite the difficulties. The local product is hardship, the bandits are fierce, the disaster situation is serious, and the suffering of the people is beyond description. In addition, volcanoes erupt frequently, and villages and towns are often in ruins, which is heartbreaking and unbearable to witness. The difference between Gansu's disaster relief and other provinces is that the political problem must be solved first. Otherwise, relief workers will not be able to carry out relief, and the disaster victims will never be relieved of their suffering due to the continuous disaster. On the way back south, I received an urgent telegram from the central government, saying that the Southeast was suffering from floods, and I rushed south to help with the relief. A few days later, I received an urgent telegram from Peiping (Beijing), saying that the disaster areas in the war zone were in urgent need of fundraising, and asked me to come to Peiping immediately to preside over everything. I took a detour to the war-torn disaster area in Baoding to make preliminary arrangements before taking a train south. The water on both sides was flooded, and the fields were submerged. The disaster situation along the Jinpu Railway was particularly tragic. The water was chest-deep, and there were no local good people to provide relief. The cries for help were unanswered. The old and weak died in ditches, and the young and strong struggled to survive. Corpses floated on the water, and the living were pale and emaciated. I asked the police at the train station and was told that some people had to fill their stomachs with one cake for four or five days. Helpless, I gave them some money and asked them to buy food to eat and wait for rescue. When I arrived in Shanghai, urgent telegrams were piled up, and representatives seeking relief followed one after another. Considering that relief could not be delayed and the true situation of the disaster needed to be known, I took a plane to Hankou to inspect. The areas around Wuhu, Anqing, and Jiujiang were a vast expanse of water, with fields submerged and houses floating. The once prosperous villages and towns had been transformed into swamps. Only the roofs and treetops were visible on the water. Corpses were floating and the stench filled the air. The surface of the Yangtze River in Hankou was both water and fire, making the situation even more tragic. The stench in the streets of Hankou made people imagine the terrible epidemic that would follow the flood. Fortunately, Wuhan relied on its former prosperity, and the disaster victims were not starving to death. Compared with other places, it was already considered lucky. After returning to Shanghai, I immediately sent a large number of staff to provide urgent relief. However, there were many obstacles during the implementation, which was difficult to achieve. Soon, I received a warning from Jiangbei, so I rushed to the Gaoyou and Shaobo areas. The people, animals, and houses had been submerged. Some of the disaster victims took boats to other places, but I don’t know how many died. Those who relied on their hometown and were eventually chased by the water waves did not know how many. Sighing and looking up at the embankment, even those on the rooftops were not safe. In short, the Southeast, which is known for its prosperity in the country, has suffered this catastrophe. Heaven's cruelty to us can be said to be both tragic and cruel. To attribute the crime and reveal the bottom line, the people cannot escape the blame. For the current plan, there are three things that need to be done urgently: first, urgent relief; second, industrial relief; and third, agricultural relief. Step by step, do it seriously, or there may be a day when the people will be relieved. Now is the time to raise funds, which is easier to arrange. In the future, when urgent relief is implemented, the funds will be ten or a hundred times more than today, and the difficulty of donating funds will also be ten or a hundred times more than today. Then, the hidden worries of the society and the future of the nation can be imagined. At this time, the country is in trouble, and the national steps are difficult. All of us Chinese people must not wake up and work hard to revitalize. It is painful for those who are close to us and pleasing to those who hate us. Imperialists are taking advantage of the situation and invading step by step. How can we resist them? How can we maintain the survival of the country and the livelihood of the people? Those who have money contribute money, and those who have no money contribute effort. Exhaust the power of the people across the country to deal with it. Although the disaster situation is great, relief has been achieved. People will conquer nature. I am willing to work hard with you all and my compatriots across the country.) (Note by the National News Agency: This article was quickly recorded by Han Mei and hastily organized, and has not been revised by Mr. Ziqiao. There may be errors, for which the reporter and Zhou Hanmei are responsible.)

Cheng Jingsheng's Work Report on the Disaster Area in Northern Jiangsu (Continued) 113

(1) The shallow water areas of the West Bank should be blocked and built solid immediately, with crushed stone slopes added, and progress should be made step by step to achieve contraction. (2) The breaches in the East Bank should be wrapped with head protection to prevent further collapse. (3) Organize the East Bank defense works. (4) Wrap the foot of the East Bank slope and make windbreaks as appropriate. (5) The East Bank breach has been leveled and the top has been cleaned up and the roads cleared to facilitate the transportation and storage of materials and to benefit the work. However, it is still not easy to plug the breach now, because there is nowhere to store materials and there is water everywhere. Now, I will divide the breaches I saw below (those within ten feet that are easy to block are excluded). (1) Two breaches of forty feet at Majia directly damaged six gates. (2) Heiyu Pond sixty feet, a total of four breaches. (3) Zhaoguan Dam more than fifty feet, the water flow is very rapid, I heard that the dam foundation has been washed away, and the waves are two miles long, pouring straight down. (4) Lotus Pond more than ninety feet, the flow is also rapid. (5) Laisheng Nunnery thirty feet, the land belongs to Lujin Weinei, 36,000 mu, the residents on the ground have been washed away. (6) Thirty Li Pu more than sixty feet, the bank behind the gate has been destroyed, and the dam will collapse one after another. There are three breaches in the West Bank, one of which is very serious. (7) Twenty Li Pu ninety feet, the water situation is dangerous. (8) Qigong Temple thirty feet, not very smooth in the past. (9) Yuma Tou forty feet, the water situation is very dangerous. (10) Miaoxiang Kou seventy feet, the water situation is extremely dangerous. Yaogunjian Building is about 170 feet long, the situation is the most dangerous, the sound of the water is turbulent, and the sound is heard for ten miles. Dozens of ships were washed down the breach and died together. Alas! In short, if the breach is not blocked for a day, the water of Hongze Lake will inevitably pour into the various counties of Yang, and the villages, towns, and cities will be turned into lakes. The saying that the West Lake moved east has unfortunately come true. It is a catastrophe that has never happened before. Chairman Ye asked Uncle Xiang to participate in the matter in person, and Uncle Gong still said that he was not sure, but after repeated appointments, he promised to transfer the appointment to Wan Xiaoan, who is also a water conservancy expert in Suzhou. Chairman Ye decided to go to Qingjiang with Uncle Gong to visit Xiao Lao in person. Jing then divided the boat with him. Director Li has been busy on the canal for several days, has already understood the situation, is brave in taking responsibility, and is doing his best to plan, which is admirable. In short, the two public officials, Ye and Li, have a compassionate heart, and those who do not take responsibility cannot be compared on the same day. That night, Jin Junxingya and Shi Junzhiying had rescued 200 refugees and transported them to Yangzhou for resettlement. On the second day of September, when the resettlement was located in the three places of Dawang Temple Chengtian Temple, etc., more than 6,000 people were rescued. Temporary resettlement was established in more than forty places, and ships were used for transportation and have been revoked. The most lacking in You and Shao are rice, food, and reeds, and telegrams have been sent to Shanghai and Yang for handling. In the morning, passing Jieshou, there was backwater five miles away, which was not very fierce. There was backwater fifteen miles away from Shuishui, which was also very peaceful. In the afternoon, a storm came from the southeast, and the backwater rose by several feet along the way. In the afternoon, I arrived at Bao Ying and met the local elders. The backwater rose sharply last night and this morning, breaking the Taiping and other embankments. The water had forced the northeast gate. A meeting was held at the Jinsheng Association, and Mr. Bao Zhizhi and others cried bitterly. In the evening, I went out of the east gate to look at the water, and only the Tongxing Embankment was not broken. Thousands of people were rushing to protect it, and the sound of evil was miserable. At night, gongs were sounded everywhere, and people were talking, because once the Tongxing Embankment was broken, there would be no clean land in the whole area. According to reports, many people died in Dongxiang. The office in Bao was hired by the association to hire sixty ships to rescue the lives. Once rescued, they should be kept together with the more than 1,000 Gaoyou refugees who have been resettled. The people in the city are in a panic, and there is a tendency to be unsustainable. On the second day, the ships still did not reply, and more than twenty were requisitioned. In the afternoon, I went south to Shuishui and asked Mr. Hua Fu to organize a resettlement center and requisition ships. In the evening, I passed Jieshou and contacted the local area and requisitioned fifty ships to rescue and resettle. On the morning of the third day, Kui Gaoyou, Director Zhu Zhongjian had arrived in Yangzhou to contact the resettlement. I did not meet him. On this day, You successively resettled more than 6,000 people. At noon, I arrived in Yangzhou. The two gentlemen Cao and Yuan had added two resettlement centers because the three places were not enough for resettlement and had requisitioned eighty ships to go to remote areas to rescue disaster victims. The kitchen utensils were complete and the office was very well-organized. At that time, I immediately decided on various measures with Cao, Yuan, and Zhu. On the morning of the fourth day, I arrived in Zhenjiang and discussed the issues of Zhenkuan Zhenpin and restoring traffic with Leng Yuqiu, Lu Xiaobo, and Director Hu. That evening, I took a night train to Shanghai.

Disaster Victims from Gaoyou and Shaobo Arrive in Shanghai 114

Yesterday, 4,000 refugees from Gaoyou and Shaobo in northern Jiangsu arrived in Shanghai and were resettled by the Shanghai Disaster Victim Resettlement Office at Chao Hui Villa. Fourteen people had gone to the Chaozhou Wuyi Villa at the South Railway Station and were also provided with accommodation and supplies by the Resettlement Office. Yesterday, reporters from the Guowen News Agency went to various places to investigate and found that the resettlement in various places had increased compared with a few days ago. The disaster victims were from the four provinces of Hubei, Jiangxi, Anhui, and Jiangsu. Other provinces have not been seen. The statistics of the number of people resettled in recent days are as follows: 16 people at the Liuying Road Resettlement Center in Zhabei, 130 people at Qu Zhenren Temple on Zhizaoju Road, 125 people at the Hunan Guild Hall on Xieqiao, 95 people at the Dongting Dongshan Guild Hall on Liyuan Road, 40 people at the Suzhou Jiyi Public Office, 24 people at the Chaozhou Wuyi Villa at the South Railway Station, 204 people at the Chao Hui Villa on Longhua Road, 63 people at the Gaochang Temple on Dananmen, 21 people at the Cuiwei Nunnery on Liuying Road in Zhabei, 40 people at the Zhejiang Jinji Shantang on Liyuan Road, and more than 40 people at the Chao Hui Villa on Longhua Road.

Investigation Report on the Disaster Situation in Jiangpu 116

The Jiangsu Flood Relief Association requested Mr. Wang Shaoyun to go to investigate the disaster situation in Jiangpu. The investigation report is excerpted below. (1) Causes of the disaster: This summer, the county has been experiencing continuous rain for ten days, and the rivers have been rising. The weirs and banks in the countryside are low and already in danger. In addition, floods broke out in Huangshan, Anhui Province, rushing to Pujing via Quanjiao, and pouring down. The water was huge, reaching several feet high. The big and small weirs and banks were all breached, and the roofs of the houses and the tops of the trees were submerged under the water. It was extremely tragic for a while. (2) Disaster-stricken areas: The county is divided into five major areas. The disaster situation is the most serious in the eastern area, followed by the northern area, then the southern and central areas, and the western area is free from disaster, only suffering slight losses during strong winds. A. Eastern area: It belongs to the Banqiao Huaqi Camp area. Among the villages in this area, Beicheng suffered the most, followed by Gao Li Yi and Er villages, and then Hua Ta Ding Nao and other villages. Beicheng is close to Anhui Province, and the mountain flood broke out, bearing the brunt. Beicheng Weir is the largest weir in the county, with a circumference of more than forty miles and about 30,000 to 40,000 mu of farmland. The weir bank was breached in eighteen places, ranging from forty to fifty feet long to more than ten feet short. In addition, the Sanlian Yueyang two weirs nearby were breached at the same time, with about 20,000 mu of farmland each, and suddenly became a swamp. Other places such as Jiqing Township, Laoyougang, and General Temple were also submerged, and they were waiting for relief. According to the Red Swastika Society's investigation report, there were more than 1,800 households. B. Northern area: It belongs to the Dongge area. This area has a larger area and the largest population. Nineteen villages were affected by the disaster, and twenty-five weirs were breached, with Kangjia Weir being the most serious, followed by Xujia Weir and Fuxing Weir. When the flood came, a large gap was washed away in the nearby mountains, about several feet wide, and there were many small gaps. The ferocity of the water can be imagined. A total of about 40,000 mu of farmland was submerged, and more than 4,000 households were affected by the disaster. C. Southern area: It belongs to the Puzhen area. Gao Wang, Changshan Bridge, Dongzun West and other places are all disasters, with more than ten weirs breached and more than 800 households affected by the disaster. They moved to Gaofu and were waiting to be fed. Since August 25 and 26, the wind was strong and the tide was high, and more were submerged. Fifteen of the sixteen villages in the area were affected by the disaster. D. Central area: The disaster situation in Jiufu Township in this area is more serious, followed by Shifo and then Luofeng. Initially, fewer than ten weirs were breached, but since the wind disaster, it has become even more widespread. The situation is similar to that in the southern area. E. Western area: This area is a mountainous area and is free from disaster, but after strong winds, Huangcaofang, Xiaoli Township, and Zhaojiaba suffered slight losses. (3) Emergency relief situation: Since the county was affected by the disaster, the Red Swastika Society organized 200 bags of flour for emergency distribution and sent a wheel to rescue more than 1,000 people. The second time, another 2,000 bags of flour and 2,000 reed mats were distributed, but only for the use of the northeastern area. In addition, various businesses in Puzhen raised more than 1,000 yuan to relieve the eastern area. The provincial government issued 5,000 yuan, which is still in the county government. It is now planned to purchase flour and distribute it in different areas. This is the general situation of emergency relief. (4) Needs for continued relief: This time, the county was flooded in various areas. At the beginning, the disaster victims could move to higher places and bring some food and utensils. When the mountain flood broke out, the high and low weirs and fields were submerged. Many disaster victims climbed trees, and those who could not escape were drifting with the current. In the eastern area alone, about two or three hundred people were drowned. The fields, houses, food, livestock, farm tools, and food were washed away. The survivors after the robbery had no home to return to and were sleeping in the open air, waiting to die. The cries for help were unbearable to hear. The water is still more than ten feet high, and it is a vast expanse of water. Looking into the distance, only the treetops can be seen. It is a catastrophe that has not happened in a hundred years. In the blink of an eye, autumn will pass and winter will come, and the water will recede. The future is long. Alas, these disaster victims have no place to live, no clothes to keep warm, and no food to eat. How can they bear it? Therefore, emergency relief is necessary today, and winter relief should not be delayed. How should we continue to raise relief funds? Please decide and implement it.

Report from Dongtai: The Water Level Continues to Rise 117

Yesterday, the Dongtai Shanghai Association received a letter from the county's temporary flood relief association, stating that the water level has increased without decreasing in recent days. The city is several feet deep in water, and boats are passing through the streets. The houses have been washed away, and people and animals have been drifting away. The warehouses have been destroyed, and the losses are incalculable. The disaster victims are clinging to trees, waiting to be rescued. The leaves of the trees have been eaten, followed by algae. The wailing is deafening, and it is unbearable to hear. The corpses are rolling and drifting downstream. The most tragic thing is that the corpses of men, women, and children are tied together with ropes, thinking that the whole family could not escape and made the decision to live together and die together. The county previously sent Liu Shaoxuan to Dafeng Yuhua to open the Beimaoyou River Dam, but the two companies still firmly resisted. However, the provincial government has telegraphed Supervisor Zhang and Director Li to allocate teams to assist, and representatives from the three counties of Taiyan have also arrived in Dongtai one after another to discuss the way out of the West Water. On the 30th, the Xiaohai people went to Wenwangjiagang to dredge the sand and at the same time demanded the opening of the Wangjiagang Fuli River in the nine counties of Xiahe, which was blocked by the gate dam of the Zhongtong Sui Company, in order to facilitate the common discharge. However, the Tong Sui Dafeng Company and other hundreds of tenant farmers colluded, holding iron forks, wooden sticks, broadswords, etc., and swarmed to intercept and attack. Now, many corpses have been found at the mouth of Wangjiagang, and the families have identified Shan Baolai and Wang Wenshou. Others are still under investigation. On the 31st, provincial government member Wu Yuanyou brought 6,000 yuan in foreign currency and 100 bags of flour to Dongtai for emergency relief. The county flood relief association discussed and decided on the following distribution methods: (1) Dry food will be distributed immediately. (2) Flour will be made into cakes, steamed buns, and other foods immediately. (3) 6,000 yuan in relief funds will be used as immigration fees for 50% and relief fees for 50%. (4) Ferries and civilian ships will be dispatched as much as possible. (5) Immigration fees will be issued after the disaster victims reach the concentration point (those leaving the county). (6) Ships will be sent out to purchase and immigrate for food. (7) Implement Ping Ti. (8) Send another telegram to the province for relief. (9) Immigrate to Jiangdu Nantong and other counties. (10) Committee member Wu and County Magistrate Huang telegraphed the three counties of Nantong Jiangdu Rugao to set up refugee shelters. (11) Relief funds and supplies will be received and distributed by this association. The Nantong County Flood Relief Group has prepared relief food, four steamers, and twenty-five civilian ships, which will be sent to Dongxing and will arrive on the 1st. On the same day, Rugao County also sent a steamer. A rescue team has been organized and divided into five groups to rescue the lives. The disaster situation is so serious that it is rare in ancient times. It is useless without a large amount of emergency relief. It is also hoped that the Sanhe Dam in Huxi will be reinforced to prevent the source. Otherwise, the eastward migration of Hongze Lake will become a reality, and the disaster will be even more unpredictable.

The Relief Committee Announces Ten Admonitions for Relief Distribution 120

Mr. Xu Shiying, concerned that relief personnel in various provinces currently engaged in urgent relief efforts might be negligent or engage in embezzlement, personally drafted ten admonitions for relief distribution. These were promulgated by the Central Relief Committee and are recorded below: (1) Know that relief distribution is the most important duty and greatest responsibility of mankind. One should dedicate one's entire body and mind to the victims, embracing a spirit of self-sacrifice and putting forth genuine effort to fulfill this serious mission. (2) Know that the lives of the victims rest on your shoulders and their survival is in your hands. (3) Know that relief funds are of utmost importance. Embezzlement and corruption are unforgivable sins and misappropriation violates national laws. (4) Know that saving the afflicted is like fighting a fire. There should be no delay or carelessness. (5) Be diligent in your own life. Be upright and conscientious. Be meticulous in your planning and efficient in your execution. (6) Always maintain a strong spirit and be thorough in your actions. Furthermore, remain calm and patient and do not be afraid of hard work. (7) Do not rely on hearsay and never delegate to others. Investigations must be thorough and precise and distributions must be meticulous and thoughtful. Every penny and every ticket must be personally delivered to the victims. (8) Immerse yourself among the victims. You must put yourself in their shoes and think from their perspective. Treat the diseases and suffering of the victims as you would the diseases and suffering of your own parents, siblings, and children. Do your best to provide assistance and do not simply consider the distribution of money and food as the end of the matter. (9) After each day's work, examine your conscience and carefully reflect on your actions. Examine yourself for any mistakes and use your personal experiences to improve relief efforts. (10) Know that one penny can save a life. Wasting one penny is tantamount to killing a life. Failure to be honest and thorough is self-destructive and goes against conscience. Sucking the marrow of the victims is like condemning your descendants to eternal suffering. The innocent children are watched over by Heaven above. Rewards and punishments will be given without fail. A single moment of carelessness will be condemned by both man and Heaven. Be vigilant and careful.

(5) Ask YMCAs in various countries to assist in fundraising. (6) Assist in investigating the situation in the disaster areas and study post-disaster problems. (7) Strictly curtail the association's budget for this year and contribute 5,000 yuan as disaster relief office expenses. In addition, telegrams have been sent to YMCAs in various overseas countries requesting assistance.

Continuing Reports on the Floods in Various Counties of Anhui 123

▲Wuhuai River in Wuhe Bursts. Floodwaters are over ten feet deep on flat ground. Dykes and embankments are collapsing in succession, houses are collapsing, and people and animals are drifting away. The disaster situation is extremely serious.

▲Lingering rain for months in Xuyi. Villages submerged account for seven-tenths of the entire county. The number of people and animals drowned and houses collapsed is even more difficult to count.

▲The Huai River in Sixian bursts. The city and countryside are a vast expanse of water. More than 14,000 people have drowned. Tens of thousands of houses have collapsed, with no distinction between high and low ground. The water is five feet deep on flat ground, and boats travel on land.

▲The water is eight feet deep on flat ground in Tianchang. Dykes and embankments have all collapsed, and the city and country streets have all become marshes.

▲Areas along the river in Chuxian have become a marsh. Over a hundred dykes and embankments have collapsed. The sounds of wailing are unbearable to hear.

▲Waves rage across over a hundred miles in Lai'an and everything has been submerged. Over fifty large and small dykes have collapsed. Over 60,000 people are displaced.

▲Over two hundred dykes have collapsed in Hexian. The disaster area is so vast that almost the entire county has been submerged. Over 200,000 people are displaced, without food or clothing. The situation is extremely dire.

Telegraphic Request Not to Send Hospital Ships to Hankou 124

Jin Baoshan, director of the Health Division of the National Government Flood Relief Committee, Dr. J.B. Grant of the Peking Union Medical College, and Dr. B. Boicic, a health expert from the League of Nations, are currently in Hankou organizing medical relief work for the Flood Relief Committee. They have telegraphed Dr. Liu Ruiheng of the Ministry of the Interior, stating that after research, the establishment of hospital ships is not suitable at all. They requested that Shanghai be consulted immediately and not to send hospital ships to Hankou, but to reorganize into land hospitals, and all the required equipment should be transported to Hankou in order to organize land hospitals. After receiving the telegram, Dr. Liu immediately notified the various groups in Shanghai organizing hospital ship affairs for consideration.

The various situations are recorded as follows:

▲Contact the inspection officer Bonn, the head of the Diplomatic Division of the International Labor Office, to assist China's factory inspection. At 2:00 p.m. on the 5th, together with Wang Renlin, acting director of the China Labor Bureau, and Fu Ganghou, chief of the Labor Protection Section of the Industrial Department, went to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau to contact Director Pan Gongzhan about factory inspection matters. It was scheduled to first inspect the Chinese and foreign factories in this city that apply the Factory Law.

▲Notify various factories that ten factory inspectors, including Niu Yinchu, have been preparing for various tasks before factory inspection at the Social Affairs Bureau for several days, which is very busy. A special notice was issued to the Chinese and foreign factories in this city that should be inspected yesterday so that they can be properly entertained when the time comes.

▲Inspection Schedule When Bonn inspected the factory, it was learned that in addition to the personnel dispatched by the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau to accompany him, the acting director of the China Labor Bureau and the chief of the Labor Protection Section of the Industrial Department also went with him. The inspection schedule is recorded as follows: Nanyang Tobacco Factory on the afternoon of the 8th, Zhabei Water and Electricity Factory on the morning of the 9th, Yong'an Textile Factory 2 in Wusong on the afternoon, Grand Kung Silk Mill on the morning of the 10th, British and American Tobacco Factory on the afternoon, Dalong Iron Factory on the morning of the 11th, Shenhe Machine Factory on the afternoon, Jiangnan Paper Mill on the morning of the 12th, Xiang Sheng Iron Factory on the afternoon, Commercial Press on the morning of the 14th, Fuxin Flour Factory 7 on the afternoon, Xinchang Silk Mill on the morning of the 15th, Zhanghua Woolen Mill and Huafeng Enamel Factory at noon, China First Knitting Factory on the morning of the 17th, Wuzhou Gubeng Factory on the afternoon, Longhua Cement Factory on the morning of the 18th,

Yesterday Was U.S. Labor Day 130

The U.S. Bridge Is Suspended for Rest

Dami Evening News said that today (7th) is U.S. Labor Day. The U.S. government has long been listed as a legal holiday. All public and private institutions in the United States are suspended for rest. The U.S. Consulate General and the Procuratorate in this city are closed for one day as usual. American foreign firms are also closed to commemorate it. Labor Day was created with the American Federation of Labor. The American Federation of Labor was initiated by Gompers, an American Jew. Gompers was originally from the United Kingdom and dedicated his life to seeking welfare for workers. After becoming an American citizen, he devoted all his energy to the labor movement. Because of his noble character and hard work, he was quickly promoted to the leader of the labor movement. He overcame all difficulties to form this association. Today, Americans may have doubts about the methods and means he used, but they all agree that his original intention was purely to seek welfare for workers, with no selfish intentions involved. Even on his deathbed, he still remembered the Federation of Labor. Therefore, every Labor Day, tens of thousands of American workers go to Gompers's tomb to pay their respects.

After the Wuhan Water Level Receded 131

The Shipping Industry Is Planning to Recover

▲Rescue Personnel Go to Hankou. The flood in Wuhan has gradually receded in recent days, but the accumulated water in the city has lasted for four weeks and has produced odors, which has a major impact on hygiene. The Doujin Hospital opened by the Japanese in Qingdao has specially organized a Doujin Rescue Team to bring medicine to Hankou to assist in rescue. The team leader, Dajiro Ishida, together with doctors Eizo Nishimura and Zhizao Chen, team member Tanuma, and nurses Yamamoto and Osumi, a total of eight people, have come to Shanghai by the Dalian Maru. Mr. Kanai of the Manchurian Railway Health Department also arrived in Shanghai with them. When they arrived in port, Wu Liande, director of the Anti-epidemic Office of the Ministry of Health in Shanghai, went to the pier to welcome them. They stayed at the Fengyang Hotel and agreed yesterday that the Doujin Hospital would take the Yueyang Maru to Hankou today, and the Xiangjiang Maru would be allocated to the team for use on the upstream line. According to Ishida, the purpose of this trip to Hankou is to treat sick refugees in Wuhan and other disaster-stricken areas who are unable to receive medical treatment for 45 days and provide them with medicines. Another team will arrive in China from Tokyo soon.

▲Pumping Accumulated Water from Various Warehouses. The lower-level goods in the warehouses of various shipping companies in Hankou are completely submerged in water, and the losses are immeasurable. There is no way to move them until recently when the water has gradually receded. Various shipping companies in this city, such as Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, and Nissin, have begun to hire a large number of workers to pump water from the flooded warehouses and clean up the goods. The companies have shipped a large number of pumps and water pumps from Shanghai to Hankou for draining warehouse water for days. Among the submerged goods, it is reported that items such as sugar, salt, and seafood are completely lost, while cloth yarn can still be auctioned for a small amount. Metal products are less damaged.

▲Foreign Vessels Compete to Transport Goods. The Japanese Yamashita Company in this city has begun to proceed in an attempt to obtain the right to transport American wheat. Various American ships in Shanghai are also considering competing to transport it. British ships are planning to transport hardware and building materials from Shanghai to Hankou. Recently, various foreign ships have been doing their best to compete for this business.

▲Ocean Vessels Transport Goods Upstream. Since the rise of the waters, the ocean vessels of the European and American lines in this city, which used to go directly to Hankou to load export goods such as mineral sand, sesame, tung oil, eggs, beans, and cotton, have all suspended their voyages. Recently, as the water has receded, the British, Japanese, and German foreign vessels in this city have proposed to restore the direct Hankou service for foreign ocean cargo to avoid transshipment at Yichang, Shashi, and Changsha. There is no difficulty for European and American goods to arrive in Hankou without warehouse storage capacity. In addition, Japan annually transports about 150 million yuan worth of raw materials for industry and commerce, such as grains, hemp, and eggs, from Hankou to Japan. This flood and boycott have greatly affected them, and they are seeking to remedy the situation.

楊 阿 囡 謀殺 親夫 嫌疑 137

屍體 有 傷痕 數 處

眞相 如何 候 偵訊

Yang Anan is suspected of murdering her husband. There are several wounds on the body. The truth remains to be investigated.

Liu Lun, the chief of the Sixth District, Third Precinct of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau in the Caojing District of Western Shanghai, learned on the 6th of this month that Yang Linxiang, a resident of Jia Yi Bridge in the 24th Tu of this district, was murdered by his wife, Yang, and immediately ordered Police Chief Zhang Bukui to conduct a detailed investigation. According to reports, the deceased Yang Linxiang's original surname was Xia. He was adopted as a son-in-law by Yang Bingsheng. Yang was 31 years old, and his wife, Yang, whose nickname is Anan, had been married to Linxiang for four years.

Anan's romantic nature caused a poor relationship between the couple. With Yang Linxiang's death, there was a consensus that she was murdered by his wife. Chief Liu, regarding this case as murder, went to investigate himself and saw that Yang Linxiang's body was moved to the parlor and lay supine on the coffin lid. Upon closer inspection, there was a purple mark on the neck, extending to behind the ear, bloodstains on the tip of the nose, a small broken skin on the forehead, and several red and blue spots on both legs. The body was swollen and already smelling. The deceased's wife, Yang Anan, was not at home, which was suspicious. He immediately ordered the local bailiff to report to the court and ordered the police to arrest the murderer. At 5:00 PM on the same day, Yang Anan was arrested and brought to the precinct. According to Yang's confession, her original surname was Xu. When she was three years old, Yang Bingsheng adopted her as his own daughter. Her husband, Yang Linxiang, entered the family as a son-in-law at the age of nine and had been married for four years. They had a son. Her adoptive father, Bingsheng, had passed away. On the third day of this month, after her husband Yang Linxiang got drunk, he suddenly

demolished the brick tomb of the adoptive father's coffin and was beaten several times by his uncle Yang Huaisheng. She entered the room at night, closed the door, and went to sleep. At eight o'clock the next morning, she still hadn't gotten up. Since she and her husband slept separately, she knocked on the door and asked him to have breakfast, but he did not respond after a long time. She pried the door open and saw that her husband had used his belt to hang himself on the

rafter wood in the room. She firmly denied the murder. Chief Liu, considering that Yang Anan was highly suspected of murder, temporarily detained her and waited for the court to verify the situation before further investigation. Yesterday (the 7th) at 1:00 PM, Prosecutor Wu Deying and Clerk Wang Mengtao of the Local Court came to examine the body. It was stated that

the body had changed and could not be determined. After the deceased's wife, Yang Anan, was sent to the court for interrogation and trial, a re-examination will be conducted to finalize the case. It was also learned that Chief Liu summoned Xia Fusan, the brother of Yang Linxiang, for questioning. According to the testimony, the deceased was his younger brother. He heard from the villagers that his sister-in-law, Yang, had a lover outside. Because they lived separately and were far away, he did not know if it was true. Today, seeing the wounds on Linxiang's body, he didn't know if he was murdered by his sister-in-law. However, rumors are frightening and he dared not say anything rashly. Chief Liu, considering that this case involved injury, decided to prepare a document today and send it to the court for interrogation and trial.

巨鼠 竟 噬 婦人 138

歷 四 小時 始 獲 捕殺

A giant rat actually bit a woman. It took four hours to capture and kill it.

Tang Xiaomei, a woman residing at 146 North Sichuan Road in this city, had her husband working on a Yangtze River liner for Jardine Matheson and was not at home. She has five sons. The night before last, her third son was already asleep when she got up to check the room. She saw a giant rat stealing the leftover rice from her youngest son's bowl. She tried to scare the giant rat away, but the rat jumped up and bit her throat, nose, and neck forcefully. She screamed in extreme pain and called for help. Neighbors and people living with her rescued her with weapons. The Zhabei Health Bureau officials, upon hearing the news, led three inspectors to the scene. After examining the scene, it took four hours to dig the rat out of the ground, kill it, and inspect it. It was found that it was not poisonous. The woman was sent to the hospital for treatment. Although she was seriously injured, her life was not in danger.

移 經懺 資助 賑 143

金山 高 吹 萬 君 之 義舉

Moving the recitation of scriptures to aid disaster relief - the righteous act of Mr. Gao Chuiwan from Jinshan.

Mr. Gao Junbin from Jinshan originally planned to hold Buddhist ceremonies in September this year to commemorate the third anniversary of the death of his grandmother, Madam Li. Now, upon the order of his father, Mr. Chuiwan, in view of the floods in the country, he is willing to transfer the 200 yuan for the ceremonies to disaster relief. The funds have been turned over to the Flood Relief Association. It is also heard that Mr. Junbin's sons and nephews, who are only three or five years old, have all donated their money for sweets to relief efforts, collecting 100 yuan, which will be sent to the charity relief organization for distribution. The original announcement of Mr. Gao is recorded below:

Oh virtuous ancestor, filial and kind, with complete roots of goodness and perfect fulfillment of blessings. The days and months do not dwell, and the third anniversary has arrived in a flash. Every festival, the sound of Sanskrit chants should be declared, relying on the great grace of my Buddha, one should ascend to the Pure Land early. Now, Heaven has brought disaster to China, and floods have caused devastation. The land is filled with wailing, and all are drowning. People are not made of wood or stone, how can they not feel compassion? Unfilial ones are willing to follow the great compassion of the former virtuous ancestor, to take the lead in rescuing those in distress. They respectfully donate 200 yuan for disaster relief, daring to hope that you will distribute it on their behalf. The former sages have said, reciting the Buddha and reciting relatives are originally one and the same. Using this to help, we use it to make do with a temple for the moment, and to keep those who are hungry alive, it can still fund blessings in the afterlife. A single grain of millet knows that it is of no help to the Ganges River, and it is appropriate to devote one's efforts for attaining the triple wisdom. Resident Chuiwan Gao Xiexun of Jinshan respectfully announces.

打胎 致 人 死命 145

兩 打胎 婦人 俯首 無 詞

判 還押 候 再 定期 宣判

Abortion leading to death. Both abortionists bow their heads silently. The sentence is postponed to another date.

On the 18th of last month at 6:00 PM, Madam Yuan from Yangzhou, a resident of 1211 Wuzhou Road, 33 years old, became pregnant due to an affair with an absconding fellow villager known as "Big Eyes." Fearing that the fetus in her womb would cause inconvenience in the future, she entrusted Madam Gao Dai, a woman from Jiangbei, to introduce Wang Chen, a skilled abortionist from the same village, to abort the fetus for three yuan. After the matter was investigated by the Harbin Police, Detective Yuan Taibin arrested Gao and Wang and sent them to the First Special District Court for questioning and detention, as reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Xiao Xiephan presided over the further trial in the Third Criminal Court. Attorney Zhang from the police station presented the case and requested investigation. Madam Liu Yushi, a woman from Yancheng, testified that she had known the deceased for many years and that Gao Dai lived with her. Yuan came and asked her to introduce Wang Chen for an abortion. Judge Xiao declared to the two defendants that the forensic doctor of this court found that Yuan died from abortion. Did they have anything to say? Both defendants bowed their heads silently and asked for leniency. The judge ordered both to be remanded in custody, awaiting a scheduled sentence.

空屋 中 自縊 男屍 146

貧 不 聊生 自殺

A man's body hangs himself in an empty house. He committed suicide because he was too poor to live.

The widening of the Ximen Yi Lane is currently underway, and all houses are being demolished. Unexpectedly, the night before last, a man's body was found hanging in an empty house. Upon learning of this from the Second District Police Station, police were dispatched to investigate. A note was found in the deceased's pocket, which read "Shi Zhifeng, residing at No. 5, Lin Jin Li, Lin Yin Road, Da Lin Road outside Xiaoximen" and two lines of poorly written poetry, explaining the reason for the suicide. The original poem reads, "It's hard for a poor youth to get through the day, that's why there's no other way." The police officer presented the report to the district chief, who ordered that his wife, Shi Wu, be summoned. She stated that her husband used to sell foreign socks, but recently because his capital was short, he could not continue his business. He had been eating away at his savings for days during the heavy rain, so he had spent all his money and became disillusioned. The district chief immediately ordered the fifth district bailiff, Dong Jianqing, to report to the local court. Prosecutor Wu and others came to the scene and determined that it was a case of death by hanging. They instructed the family to collect the body for burial. If they were unable to do so, the bailiff was ordered to report to the authorities to arrange for burial.

服毒 旅客 之 查明 148

王志魁 實 係 沈嘉泰

用空 公 欵 無法 彌補

Identity confirmed of the traveler who took poison. Wang Zhikui is actually Shen Jiatai. Public funds were used up and could not be compensated.

On the evening of the third, Wang Zhikui, who claimed to be a native of Suzhou doing business in foreign goods, checked into a room at the Nanjing Hotel in the French Concession and committed suicide by swallowing raw opium. The bellboy heard moaning and reported it to the police station. He was taken to Renji Hospital for treatment but died. The body was verified by the court. Because there was no way to investigate the family of the deceased, it was ordered that the body be collected by Tongren Fuyu Tang. It is now learned that the real name of the deceased is Shen Jiatai, 28 years old, from Nanxiang, who worked as a clerk at HSBC Bank. He usually liked gambling. He was already married and had children. Seven years ago, he wanted to commit suicide by jumping into the sea at Wusong Paotaiwan because of debt, but his wife found out and chased him back halfway. Recently, because he used up the funds in the bank and could not compensate for it, he had a short-sighted view and committed suicide by taking poison. His father, Shen Chunfu, works at the Zhabei Charity Group and lives at No. 470 Fangbang Road. Yesterday, his father learned about it and rushed to the mortuary with his wife to identify the body. However, the body had already been collected, so he immediately requested it back, purchased clothes and a coffin, replaced the coffin, and transported it back to his hometown for burial.

愚園路 溺斃 女屍 之 相騐 149

The examination of the female corpse drowned on Yuyuan Road.

The Nanjia Lane area of the Twelfth Tu of the Twenty-eighth Bao of Western Shanghai's Yuyuan Road is located in a remote and desolate area, and pedestrians rarely set foot there. There are only a few tall Western-style houses standing there. Yesterday morning at about 8:00 AM, the residents of the Western-style house suddenly smelled a foul odor that made people sick. They opened the window on the upper floor and looked around and suddenly saw an unnamed female corpse floating on the surface of a small stream (named Lujia Creek) next to the house. It seemed to have rotted. They immediately sent someone to report to the Jing'an Temple Police Station, considering that it hindered hygiene and involved a human life. The police chief, because the place belonged to the Chinese territory, sent a detective to the Sixth District Police Station. After receiving the report, District Chief Ren sent Inspector Xu to investigate. It was found that the female corpse was about thirty years old, wearing a black foreign cloth shirt and pants, with her hair in a bun, and a bunch of keys beside her. She looked like a woman from Jiangbei. Her entire body had rotted, and several inches of large intestine flowed out of her lower body. It was presumed that she had fallen into the water and died from drowning about three or four days ago. After inspecting the scene, he immediately ordered the bailiff of the Tu, Sheng Xiangzhou, to report to the local court and request that someone be sent to examine the body. At about 4:00 PM, Prosecutor Wu, appointed by the court, brought a forensic officer to the scene to examine the body. It was found that the unnamed female corpse had indeed drowned after falling into the water. Because there was no way to find the family of the deceased, he ordered the bailiff of the Tu to prepare a coffin, collect the body, and bury it.

潘 湘 娥 堅 欲 離婚 150

Pan Xiang'e insists on divorce.

Pan Xiang'e, the eldest daughter of Pan Guoliang, a local resident of No. 5 Yonglu Lane, Baxianqiao, French Concession, is 25 years old this year. She married Zhang Muqing's son Zhang Yiling of Zhenjiang at the age of sixteen. They have three sons and one daughter. Due to unbearable abuse, she returned to her mother's home in the winter of last year. Recently, she hired a lawyer to file a petition to the Civil Mediation Court of the Second Special District, requesting mediation and separation from her husband. Because the mediation failed, she has now formally filed a lawsuit, requesting a judgment for separation, and demanding that the defendant pay 2,880 yuan in living expenses for two years (120 yuan per month), 400 yuan to repay the expenses for returning to her mother's home for eight months, and 500 yuan in savings and 45 yuan in interest, totaling 3,825 yuan. However, she is unable to pay the litigation fee and requests assistance. Yesterday, Judge Pang Shurong summoned both parties to the case to investigate the litigation assistance and mediate. He ordered the parents of both parties to appear in court and repeatedly persuaded them to make concessions and return to harmonious cohabitation. However, Zhang Pan Xiang'e firmly refused. Regarding the litigation fee, she requested permission to guarantee assistance and pay it after the case is closed. The judge, seeing that persuasion was ineffective, ordered them to leave and wait for verification.

The two packages of opium on the rickshaw.

法 捕房 正 探目 魯 錦臣 副 探目 王 如 松 於 昨日 上午 十 時 率領 包 探 出外 巡緝 至 永安 街 地方 查見 有 黄包車 一輛 上 載 蒲包 二 只 無人 乘坐 形跡 可疑 上前 搜查 包 内 俱是 烟土 訊 之 車夫 帶 土人 已 逃逸 當 將 烟土 帶入 捕房 權 之 計 重 七十九 磅 即 解送 第二 特區 法院 請示 先由 捕房 裨 師 顧 守 熙 陳明 案情 將 烟土 呈案 又 據 承辦 包 探 禀明 查獲 情形 推事 馬 壽 南 當庭 宣判 烟土 没收

Lu Jinchen, the chief detective of the French police, and Wang Rusong, the deputy detective, led detectives on patrol outside yesterday morning at 10 o'clock. At Yongan Street, they saw a rickshaw carrying two cattail bags with no one riding in it, and its appearance was suspicious. They stepped forward to search, and the bags were full of opium. When they questioned the rickshaw puller, the opium carriers had already escaped. They immediately took the opium to the police station, weighed it, and it weighed 79 pounds. 縣 財政 局長 王 華 照 昨 宣誓 就職 153

财 厅 派 嚴 愼 予 監誓

County Finance Bureau Chief Wang Huazhao was sworn in yesterday. The Department of Finance sent Yan Shenyu to supervise the oath.

Wang Huazhao, Director of the Shanghai County Finance Bureau, held a supplementary oath ceremony on the second floor of the County Government at 2:00 PM yesterday. The provincial department sent Yan Shenyu, the magistrate of Shanghai County, to represent and supervise the oath. Dozens of representatives and guests attended the ceremony. After Director Wang took the oath, the supervisor gave a speech, saying, "I am here as both a representative of the Department of Finance and in connection with the county government. The matter of finance, in today's terms, can simply be said to be having finances without politics. Today's ceremony for Director Wang is also a formality that does not supplement reality, but now that we are in this position, we on the one hand must work hard to manage finances, but on the other hand, we must do it practically and not be empty. For all matters related to finance, it is best to establish a budget in advance, and the budget must be carefully reviewed so that it does not exceed the scope, because exceeding the budget will lead to difficulties in completing the project and in developing it." Then, Jiang Yanqiu, representative of the County Party Department, Sun Shengzeng, Director of the Construction Bureau, Zhang Junpu of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, and Shi She of the Education Bureau gave speeches one after another. Director Wang replied, "The biggest income in finance is of course the land tax, but the land tax is fixed and the career is infinite. In terms of construction, it can be said that construction begins with destruction, but in terms of finance, there is only construction and no destruction. Therefore, it is really difficult to use the fixed income to run the unlimited career. In the future, I will only follow the rules of the predecessors and follow the gentlemen to work hard. On the one hand, I still need you to teach me generously in order to seek new developments, so that Shanghai's finances do not have the danger of going off track." The meeting adjourned after the speech.

公用 局 注意 本市 水源 154

令 水廠 加重 消毒

The Public Utilities Bureau pays attention to the city's water source. Orders the water plant to increase disinfection.

The Municipal Public Utilities Bureau believes that the water in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River contains a lot of toxic substances due to the recent floods, which flow downstream and inevitably affect the city's water source. The two water plants in the city, the mainland and Zhabei, both draw water from the Huangpu River. If it contains toxic substances, it will be a great danger to the health of the citizens. Therefore, it sent a letter to the Health Bureau to quickly plan special disinfection methods for the water to be followed. It is now heard that the Health Bureau has ordered the two water plants to follow the following three points: (1) Use more alum for sedimentation; (2) Frequently wash and change the fine sand in the filter pool; (3) Disinfect the clear water with salt water and conduct strict inspections at any time to emphasize drinking.

Reader's Letters

Message from Mr. Xu Zhiping

(1) In recent years, the call to go to the Northwest and the Northeast has been overwhelming. However, what is the specific plan? Is going to the frontier limited to the working class, or are people in the higher intellectual circles also going?

Regarding the publication of plans to address this issue, and if the latter also has the possibility or necessity to go, I would like to ask how to proceed (specifically regarding those who specialize in social sciences). If there are any books available on the market for reference, please also let me know.

(2) The phenomenon of economic recession has almost permeated the globe. However, because our country's politics are not on track, wars are frequent, and natural disasters are adding to the chaos, the people are struggling to survive. This situation is even more dire. How many of those who received a university education in the past have now become unemployed, high-level vagrants? The solution to this problem is also one of the things that your newspaper declares it wants to contribute to society. However, I have heard people say that there are indeed young people today who can run businesses independently without seeking help from others, such as import and export business. However, I think that to run an import business, one must have considerable knowledge and means, otherwise failure can be expected immediately. Now, I ask, is this reliable? If so, how can one obtain that knowledge? Also, are there any other businesses that one can operate independently without seeking help from others?

(Reply) Laborers can immigrate to the Northeast, and so can intellectuals. However, immigration requires a whole plan, where to move the surplus population from, where to move it to, travel expenses, and reclamation expenses must all have concrete plans. Scattered resettlement is definitely not possible. There are many things that can be done in the frontier, the most important of which is the education of immigrants, which is waiting to be launched. As long as you have a diligent and hardworking spirit, you will not have to worry about having nothing to do in the vast virgin lands of the Northeast. If you are interested in going, you can first investigate publications, such as the China Eastern Economic Monthly, published by the China Eastern Railway Bureau in Harbin, which has a lot of substantive material on immigration issues and can be subscribed to for reference.

Running an import and export business, as you mentioned in your letter, requires considerable specialized knowledge and skills. You cannot engage in it blindly. In today's China, there are many things to be done. You should choose one thing according to your own strengths and do it step by step, starting from a very small scope. Do not be greedy for quick results.

Postage Stamp for Correspondence

The Business Community's Inspection Association Regularly Establishes Inspection Teams 159

Two Steps Decided Yesterday

Completely Resist the Transit of Goods with Special Levy

The inspection work of the Anti-Japanese Aid-the-Compatriots Association has been taken over by the business community. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce's Inspection of Japanese Goods Association has already decided last week to organize inspection teams for various industries before the 10th of this month to carry out the work of resisting Japanese goods and has also passed inspection rules. The news of each item is recorded as follows:

▲ Standing Committee of the Anti-Japanese Association The Anti-Japanese Aid-the-Compatriots Committee held its 15th standing committee meeting at 2:00 PM yesterday. The committee members present were Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yansong, Tao Baichuan, Hou Dachun, and Lu Jingshi. Wang Yansong was elected as chairman. The following important cases were resolved: (1) Discussing the Wu County Anti-Japanese Association's letter requesting to bring in an industrial fund, it was decided to reply that it was difficult to do so. (2) Discussing Secretary Feng's report, that the association's method of verifying and issuing cotton yarn passes has been reviewed and completed, please pass the case. It was decided to submit it to the Executive Committee. (3) Discussing the proposal of the Custody Section regarding whether insurance, stacking and unloading, and warehouse rental fees should be recovered from the owners when releasing goods, please make a public decision. It was decided to recover it from the owners. (4) Discussing the case of Yongcheng Cloth Factory forging account books to seek registration, it was decided to revoke the registration. (5) Discussing the case of Huafeng Industrial Raw Materials Company falsely reporting the number of goods to apply for passes, it was decided that the visitor had not acted seriously enough. (6) Discussing the release of goods and passage of various goods, it was decided to handle them separately.

▲ Business Community Talk The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce's Japanese Goods Inspection Committee convened a talk yesterday with the business community of this city to discuss the progress of the work of the inspection teams for various industries. More than 100 representatives from various industries attended. Chairman Ye Jiaxing reported that the purpose of convening this talk was based on the decision made at the plenary meeting of the Inspection Committee on September 5th, believing that this economic severance of relations with Japan would adopt methods of resisting goods. However, this resistance to goods is slightly different from the past. Because our industrial and commercial circles are at the forefront of the economy, and in view of the past lessons, the current resistance to goods must be carried out according to two principles: one is to use chronic resistance to Japanese goods as a temporary solution, and the other is to use acute promotion of domestic goods as a fundamental solution. According to these two goals, we will proceed simultaneously to achieve a thorough solution. Therefore, the Anti-Japanese Association is drafting a five-year plan to ensure that Japanese goods are eliminated on the one hand, and that our country's industrial and commercial circles have a way to remedy the situation on the other. Now, speaking of resisting goods, the goods imported from Japan to our country can be divided into four types: (1) luxury goods, (2) general goods, (3) necessities, and (4) industrial raw materials. Among these four types of goods, in addition to the first two types, which are purely for consumption, should be strictly and absolutely resisted. The latter two types, from a factual point of view, cannot but be temporarily transported with a small levy before our country's domestic products can fully supply them, and the funds obtained from the levy will be used as preparations for our industrial and commercial circles to establish industries in the future. This matter is closely related to our industrial and commercial circles, and our industrial and commercial circles share the same hatred of the enemy and dare not lag behind others in their patriotism. Therefore, the association convened a temporary member meeting on July 24th and decided on the spot that our industrial and commercial circles would automatically resist Japanese goods and passed the organization of two committees for resisting goods research and inspection. Since the beginning of the process, we have been working hard and dare not slack off. Recently, the matter of inspecting Japanese goods, due to the variety of Japanese products and the situation of their import, is directly related to our industrial and commercial circles, so we know it more clearly. Therefore, at the plenary meeting of the Inspection Committee on the 5th, we proposed the method of organizing inspection teams for various industries, using the spirit of self-governance to encourage each other, and it was decided to start work on the 10th of this month. However, this matter is of great importance, and we deeply hope that our colleagues in the industrial and commercial circles will express their opinions to collect ideas and benefit widely. This is our sincere hope. As for the inspection team's rules, they have been drafted and sent to the printer. Once printed, they will be distributed to various industries for reference. Next, Qiu Liangyu, the director of the inspection team, reported that the establishment of the Chamber of Commerce's Inspection Committee is actually to strengthen the power of the Anti-Japanese Aid-the-Compatriots. Because the entire organization of the Anti-Japanese Aid-the-Compatriots, the inspection of resisting goods is a local work of the anti-Japanese movement, and the resistance of goods is mainly based on goods, and the situation of goods is known more clearly by our industrial and commercial circles. Today, when we automatically resist Japanese goods, the inspection work will be handled automatically by our industrial and commercial circles, which is also more cordial. Next, representatives from the medicine, sugar, clock and watch, mercerized cotton weaving, and other industries put forward many opinions. Because they must wait for the Inspection Committee to discuss before deciding on the proposal, it is temporarily kept secret. The inspection team's rules have been obtained and published on the left.

▲ Rules of the Inspection Association The rules of the Inspection Teams for Various Industries of the Business Community's Japanese Goods Inspection Committee: (Article 1) The inspection team is based on the principle of merchants automatically resisting goods, and its purpose is to eliminate Japanese goods from the same industry in the shortest possible time. (Article 2) The inspection team is organized by the entire committee of the industry's association, named the Business Community's Japanese Goods Inspection Committee, ○○ Industry Inspection Team. (A) The chairman of the industry's association is the director of the team. (B) All executive committee members of the industry's association are members. (C) Representatives of the members of the industry's association are members. (D) The staff within the team are concurrently held by the committee members of the industry's association. (Article 3) The powers of the inspection team are limited to the scope of the same industry. For the sale of Japanese goods by other industries, report them to the Japanese Goods Inspection Committee as much as possible, and do not directly inspect or investigate to avoid disputes. (Article 4) The powers of the inspection team are as follows: (A) Propaganda matters related to the same industry. (B) Matters of accusation related to the same industry. (C) Matters of investigation related to the same industry. Matters of review related to the same industry. (D) Matters of inspection related to the same industry. (Article 5) If there is any doubt about the identification of goods by the inspection team, it should immediately report to the Japanese Goods Inspection Committee to send someone to review. (Article 6) Japanese goods inspected by the inspection team should be sent to the Japanese Goods Inspection Committee and transferred to the Anti-Japanese Aid-the-Compatriots Association for handling, and shall not be disposed of by itself. (Article 7) If the inspection team recognizes that the sale of Japanese goods by the same industry has obstacles and it is inconvenient to exercise its powers, it should immediately make a secret report to the Japanese Goods Inspection Committee and must not remain silent. (Article 8) The inspection team should prepare a work report every month and send it to the Japanese Goods Inspection Committee for record before the 5th of the following month. (Article 9) Team meetings should be held at least once a week. The number of attendees is not fixed. Sometimes, due to business connections, this team and that team can also hold joint meetings, but they must report to the Japanese Goods Inspection Committee in advance and ask them to send someone to attend. (Article 10) If the inspection team can eliminate Japanese goods in the same industry in the shortest possible time and is verified by the Japanese Goods Inspection Committee, it may invite various honors and awards. The award method will be determined separately. (Article 11) If the inspection team's work is not effective or there are cases of favoritism, once found out, in addition to the goods being confiscated and the owner handled in accordance with the regulations of the Anti-Japanese Aid-the-Compatriots Association, the responsible personnel in the team will also be given joint and several punishments. The punishment regulations will be determined separately. (Article 12) These rules will be submitted to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for record and implementation after being passed by the plenary meeting of the Japanese Goods Inspection Committee. (Article 13) If there are any matters not covered in these rules, they may be resolved and amended by the standing committee of the Inspection Committee.

Prior Inspection and Prevention

Temporary Measures for Emergency Repair

Letter

To Whom It May Concern, The news item (Guohua Electrical Appliance Store Sued) published in your newspaper on the 7th of this month is completely inconsistent with the facts. It has been found that the Shanghai-Suzhou Guohua Electrical Appliance Store has illegally established a radio station without legal procedures, and has mixed and used the international radio station call sign (XGK XGK), and has interfered with the stations of this bureau. Therefore, in accordance with the provisions of Article 21 of the Telecommunications Regulations, the Ministry of Transportation has confiscated all its machinery and accessories, and must also impose a fine of more than 50 yuan to 2,000 yuan. After being ordered by this bureau, the case has been referred to the court for legal handling, and the court has repeatedly opened a trial. The industry has already admitted this without denying it. As for the various sections mentioned by the industry's lawyer during the court hearing, they have all been refuted by the representative of this bureau. We are now afraid that the outside world does not know the truth, and we would like to make the following clarifications: (1) (There are more than 20 companies besides Guohua in Shanghai that install radio broadcasting machines. Why are the others not investigated and only Guohua is investigated?) It has been found that this question has gone beyond the scope of this case. Guohua's private establishment of a radio broadcasting station should be dealt with according to law, and there is no excuse to escape it. (2) (Is it because Guohua Wireless in Suzhou disturbed the international radio waves and mistakenly affected Guohua in Shanghai?) It has been found that both the private establishment of radio broadcasting stations by Guohua Electrical Stores in Shanghai and Suzhou violate the provisions of the Telecommunications Regulations, and they have been strictly banned separately, and there is no misunderstanding. In view of the above two points, we hope that you will publish them in your newspaper's letter column to clarify the truth and avoid confusion. Sincerely, to the editor of Shen Bao, from the International Telecommunications Bureau of the Ministry of Transportation, September 7.
