Bushaoting Cao Zhai's Conversations

The Troubles Caused by the Solar Calendar 173

Daiyu's burial flower poem says: (Three hundred and sixty days a year, wind, knife, frost, and sword closely persecute.) This is the ordinary Chinese people's view of the year. People from the Qin Dynasty to the present have said that a year has three hundred and sixty-five days. In fact, this common spoken language is incorrect. The time required for the earth to revolve around the sun is 365 days, 5 hours, 48 minutes, and 50 seconds. We have now changed to the solar calendar, and we can no longer ignore the remainder of 5 hours, 48 minutes, and 50 seconds as we did before. The Egyptians and Romans initially calculated a year as only 365 days, omitting the remainder. The difference of a hair's breadth leads to a difference of a thousand miles. Every four years there is a difference of one day, every forty years there is a difference of ten days, and every four hundred years there is a difference of one hundred days. Over time, the seasons are all turned upside down. When the time came for change, the seasons were off by about eighty days. He corrected it in 46 BC. That year, he set fourteen months, 445 days, which is the longest year in history. This is a way to make up for previous deficiencies. From that year onwards, he determined that every four years would have a leap day, adding this day to the number of days in February. Roman customs only allowed February to have 28 days, and even Caesar's autocracy did not dare to change it arbitrarily, so February in ordinary years was always 28 days. Other months had 31 days in large months and 30 days in small months. Leap years now appear to have 29 days in February. But according to the Romans, this added day was called the day before March, not the 29th of February, so the Roman custom of February having 28 days deceived Caesar. After Caesar, the calendar was managed by the Pontiff. They messed up the calendar, having a leap year every three years. In thirty-six years, there were three extra leap days. Augustus corrected it for him. He was a man who loved fame. Seeing that July was named after Julius Caesar and was a large month, he called August by his own name, Augustus, and changed the small month to a large month, causing the order of the months to be disrupted by him. But Caesar's method of having a leap day every four years was inevitably a little long. Because four times 5 hours, 48 minutes, and 50 seconds is only 23 hours, 15 minutes, and 20 seconds. Each year there is an extra 11 minutes and 10 seconds, and in 128 years there will be an extra day. Year after year, the accumulation reached Gregory VIII (1583), and ten days had already been added. So he set October 5, 1583, as October 15 and pushed it all the way to the end of the year. In order to prevent this kind of error from happening again in the future, he stipulated that all century years, such as 1900, 2000, 2100, and 2200, should have the last two circles removed, and those that can be divided evenly by four will have a leap day, and those that cannot be divided evenly will not have a leap year. In this way, three leap years are reduced in four hundred years. But Gregory VIII's correction cannot be considered thorough, because there are still two or three days of error in ten thousand years.

Memorial Record of Premier's Statue Base 174

— Shi Yan Ye

I pass by the base of the Premier's bronze statue outside the North Station gate every week, once or twice. Neither wind nor rain can stop me. Each time I pass, I linger, paying my respects with a sigh, tears welling up. For it has been long since the cornerstone of our Premier's statue was laid. Yet the towering statue, to be revered by all, is still not to be seen. Only the square foot of stone, lying horizontally and vertically, is buried in the overgrown weeds. Although surrounded by an iron fence, inaccessible to people, the withered grass is covered with discarded batting, scraps of paper, and all sorts of filthy things, almost like a place to hide dirt and receive filth. Sometimes, one even sees trousers of a calf drying at the end of a horizontal pole on the fence. The foundation of a respected Premier's bronze statue, in the North Station, which is observed by all, is so dilapidated, and the statue has not been built for so long. Is this not lamentable? This is why I sigh every time I pass. I remember the grand ceremony of the cornerstone laying in the past. I also participated in the grand event, listening to the great speeches of those who ascended the platform. It seemed that the statue could certainly be completed in the shortest period. Who would have known that seasons have changed repeatedly, yet it is still just a base? Later, due to the shame of insufficient funds, Chen Ying Shi, for his contributions to the party and the nation, has a memorial tower towering on West Gate Road. Zhao Tie Qiao, for his work in reorganizing the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, has a bronze statue erected on the Huang Xie Pu Riverbank. Is it possible that, in the eyes of the people of Shanghai, the great personality and merits of our Premier are still below those of Chen and Zhao? Alas.

Moon Over the Parapet 175

World Tidbits 176

▲ Lobster Strangles a Mouse to Death In Paris, the capital of France, there is a central market, Cen tral Markets, which is the hub of the vegetable market. One day, a fish and shrimp vendor had a basket of lobsters. Suddenly, a large mouse came, hoping to find some good things to have a hearty meal. Who knew that there was a lobster in the basket. While the mouse was slowly crawling, the lobster suddenly stretched out its two big claws and grabbed its head and neck. Before long, it strangled the mouse to death. For a time, people in the market spread it as a strange event.

▲ Modern Cave Dwellers Near Stourbridge in Worcestershire, England, there is a small village called Kinver. Most of the village consists of sandy rocky rocks, like artificial rockeries piled up. If the villagers want to build houses on the flat ground, they have to remove these rocks. However, this is impossible. So they made the best of it, hollowing out the rocks and turning them into the shape of houses, fitting them with windows and doors, and living inside. On the contrary, they saved a batch of labor and materials for building houses. (Hai Ke)

Remembering a Couplet Lamenting Mr. Jiang Baiqi 177

— Zi Sou

Mr. Zhou Nangai is an old comrade of the Republican Party. He is proficient in history, skilled in poetry and prose. His book, Notes from the Qilan Jing She Studio, contains many anecdotes. Since the Republic, it records inside stories and anecdotes of politics in the government and among the people, but he keeps them secret and does not show them to others. He laughs and says that I am verbally insincere, or perhaps it will be after my death. Within thirty years, it is not time to publish it. In the past, those who had seen it all praised its careful judgment and strictness. The events are supported by evidence. Using the note-taking style, it secretly records historical methods. It can use the small to imply the large, and use the simple to control the complex. His talent and knowledge are both high, and his learning is especially profound. It is a work that will surely be passed down. Occasionally, one or two excerpts are circulated, but they are merely rare glimpses. For example, the record of Su Manshu was collected and published by Shou Juan Guang Sheng in the Bi-Monthly Magazine. Later, when Liu Yazi and his son compiled the Complete Works of Manshu, because it was different from the records of other people at the time and the relationship was not shallow. (This shows the great insight of the Liu family). He did not hesitate to personally visit the people mentioned in the record to inquire in detail. (This shows the thoroughness of the Liu family). They all said that it was consistent with the facts. Therefore, it was included in the Complete Works, and two poems by Zhou lamenting Su were included. Such as "Friends still have tears, the world is already without spring. Bones are decayed, and fame stands empty, the heart is hurt, and death is regretted," which were recited for a time. Mr. Jiang Baiqi rushed about for the revolution and opened a government in the southeast. His actions and words were related to the political situation, and the case in the late winter attracted worldwide attention. He recently passed away at sea, and there were many elegies. Yesterday, I saw a couplet by Zhou, saying:

(Running around for the Party and the nation, trying to save the comrades of the past. Those who were generous and kind often suffered hardship.) (Weary at the river pass, still troubled by a last letter. Full of bloody words, forever recording the hardships.) Especially I don't know what he wrote in his last letter. I think it has already become a resource in the secret history. Zhou's poems and articles are treasured and kept secret, and his words are not uttered rashly. His saying "forever record" and "bloody words" must be related and have the value of being passed down. (Uncompensated)

Record of Ziyi Inkpad 178

— Xi Zhe

For anything that is expected to be passed down, one must concentrate on its path, and then one can achieve great results. Although inkpad is a minor art, it must undergo a long period of research and dedicated effort before it can reach a wonderful state. The making of inkpad has three essentials: first, the oil must be dry and not seeping; second, the cinnabar must be red and not dark; and third, the down must be fine and not broken. If the research and preparation are done properly, then the color will be fresh and thick, the mud will be smooth and moist, there will be a sound when it leaves the paper, and the imprint will be deep and fine. Only then will the inkpad have all its capabilities. Among the inkpads that have a reputation in the world, in the past, there was only the Lihua Zhai in Zhangzhou, Fujian, and now there is only the Xiling Seal Society in Hangzhou. Although there are many other makers, they always seem to lose this and gain that, and they are not fully prepared. Mr. Xia Ziyi of Shanghai has a special love for tea and inkpad making. Every day, besides dealing with teacups, he also uses inkpad making as a pastime. He has spent decades of focused effort on refining oil, selecting sand, and making down, and has unique insights. He does not spare money or effort, and does not seek profit. Therefore, the inkpad he makes is better than the two mentioned above. I also have a fondness for this, and I once selected his newly made Chensha Ousi Divine Inkpad. After trying it, it was exquisitely unparalleled. Compared with inkpads made by other families, it is more than a hundred times better. It can be said to be an unprecedented invention. Its color is pure, not purple, not yellow, like a beautiful woman applying powder to her face and then adding rouge. It is red, tender, and moist, with a kind of ancient elegance that makes people feel relaxed. All three of the aforementioned essentials are fully prepared. Calling it a divine product is truly not an exaggeration. And Mr. Xia's dedicated and focused work will benefit the art world and be forever recorded in the history of inkpads. Therefore, I specially record it to promote it.

▲ Letter to the Editor Dear Sir, I read Zhu Ji's biography in the "Free Talk" on the 4th, which said: "A certain famous actor played Farewell My Concubine, and mistakenly pronounced 苧 (ning) in 苧蘿村 (Ningluo Village) as 丁 (ding)." According to my understanding, Ningluo Village is the hometown of Xi Shi. There are lyrics about it in the Xi Shi play, which has nothing to do with Farewell My Concubine. There is absolutely no Ningluo Binwang in Farewell My Concubine. Moreover, both Farewell My Concubine and Xi Shi were compiled and performed by Mei Lanfang. The "certain famous actor" refers to Mr. Mei, so Mr. Mei is not illiterate. And both plays have been directed by men of letters. I have traveled north and south and have been to many theaters. I have never heard him read 苧 as 丁. As for Farewell My Concubine not containing the words 苧蘿, that is fundamentally wrong. I think the writer must have misremembered. I am specially correcting it on your behalf. Please publish it in the "Letters to the Editor" column to avoid spreading misinformation. Respectfully submitted to the editorial department of Free Talk, Zhou Meijun, September 6th.

Chatting at Di Xiang Zhai 179

— Gan Yi

Pei Jingfu

Pei Boqian (Jingfu) is a native of Anhui. He served as a magistrate in Guangdong for a long time. Some people said that he could resolve a trial with a few words, revealing the truth and falsehood, and clarifying right and wrong. I also thought he was a talented man. When Ni Danchen (Sichong) was in power during Yuan Shikai's reign, he led the so-called Anwu Army to garrison northern Anhui, holding both military and political power. Pei Jingfu was in charge of political affairs, and he consulted him on everything, no matter how big or small. Jingfu followed the crowd and only said yes, without the courage he had in the past. Many people found it strange. Fu said, "I am old. I can't help but worry about my children and grandchildren. I dare not do anything illegal." Once, he went to Beijing for something. One night, he attended a banquet hosted by Yang Jiqing (Shicong). Wang Jixun (Ruikai) was present. Jingfu, drunk, spoke loudly, saying, "Hongxian is rising. Yuan Shikai can be compared to Cao Cao. Who is Cao Pi? I am afraid that it will not be like Qin, which perished in the second generation." Yang and Wang were both speechless. The next morning, Ruikai told Zhang Zhongren (Yi) about what he had said. Yi said, "Boqian's words are what I wanted to say but dared not say. Can you arrange for him to come to my humble residence for a chat?" Ruikai remained silent. Just then, Yuan Shikai summoned Yi to discuss important matters. Yi immediately said, "Does the President know that there are officials in charge of the army who criticize the monarchy?" Yuan Shikai was surprised and asked, "Who is it?" Yi said, "Ni Sichong." Yuan Shikai replied, "What does he mean?" Yi said, "Who can be Cao Pi to succeed Cao Cao?" Yuan Shikai laughed and said, "Danchen is a soldier. How can he say such things? Someone must be using his name to say what they want to say. I think it's you, my son?" Yi's face changed. Knowing that he could not hide it, he stammered, "Pei Boqian once said this, saying that Danchen really meant it." Yuan Shikai said, "Boqian is an acquaintance. You can ask him to come and see me." Yi said yes and retreated. He rushed to Ruikai's place, and they agreed to go to Jingfu's residence together to explain the matter. Fu was terrified. He packed up and left the capital overnight. Before leaving, he gnashed his teeth and said, "I almost lost my life because of Wang and Zhang's indiscreet words."

Novelty Publishing Society

A Husband's Wife (7) 180

— Jiang Hongjiao

But she knew very well in her heart, and her entire spirit was longing for her husband's return. She wanted to go up to look for him, but she was afraid of going the wrong way at the fork in the road; she thought about calling the neighbors who had a telephone to inquire at the homes of familiar relatives and friends, but because it was too late, the families with telephones had closed their doors and were sleeping quietly. She worried that her husband might be drunk and fall in the snow, or be hit by a car on the road, or be robbed and injured by thieves. She thought of everything.

Finally, a car was coming towards this side in the distance. Mr. Li had really returned. But there seemed to be a woman in the car, very beautiful and very young. Who was it? Was it his lover? Mrs. Li hurriedly hid in the darkness, watching him hold hands with that woman, watching him slowly get out of the car, and even hearing the woman say to her husband: "Come earlier tomorrow and wait for you to have dinner." The car door closed and drove away, and he was still standing there waving to the car. He pulled up the leather collar of his leather coat and wrapped it tightly around himself before starting to call the gatekeeper to open the door.

She was extremely angry and regretted waiting for him here and seeing such an unfortunate thing. She only felt that everything suddenly turned black in front of her, and she couldn't hear or see anything, and fell to the snow.

The gatekeeper opened the inner gate and let him in.

"You're back!" The gatekeeper seemed a little indignant and said very impolitely.

"Oh!" Mr. Li made a sound in his nose and walked away.

"Where's Mrs. Li?" The gatekeeper stopped him.

"What are you asking for?" Mr. Li was a little angry.

"Mrs. Li was just standing in the snow waiting for you. I advised her to go home, but she refused. When I locked the door, she was still standing on the road. Maybe she went to find you."

"She's alone?"

"Yes." The gatekeeper shined a flashlight around the alley. Mr. Li was also a little embarrassed and hurried out of the alley to look for her.

"Oh no! Something bad happened! Mrs. Li fell here!" the gatekeeper shouted. Mr. Li hurried over to look and, sure enough, it was his wife. He couldn't think of a way to rescue her, so he could only pick her up. He called the gatekeeper to shine the light and first went to knock on the door of his house. He poured brandy into her mouth and rubbed her body. Mr. and Mrs. Chen and the servants of the house also all got up to help with the rescue. It wasn't until dawn that she woke up. Besides crying loudly, she didn't say anything.

Food Grain, Downriver Rice Market Rises and Falls 190

▲South City Rice Situation The source of supply from the west yesterday was slightly connected. Retail sales in cities and towns still slowed down as the weather cleared, and customer intentions to purchase weakened, only picking top-quality goods. The price of thick japonica rice decreased by two chi, while thin indica rice was slightly available. Customer purchases were stagnant, and the local market also turned dull. However, the special edge goods were scarce and the demand was still acceptable, so the price was temporarily set. The supply of Lu Yang sharp rice was scarce and the demand was flat, so the market had no special changes. The arrival of new japonica rice and new customer sharp rice was continuous, but sales were sluggish, so the market slightly declined. A change in the weather will affect both incoming shipments and sales, which remains stable.

▲Zhabei Yesterday, there was a lack of incoming shipments of northern japonica rice from Changshu, Kunshan, and other places along the Suzhou River in the morning. By the afternoon, when the wind stopped, there were twelve or thirteen shipments. There were also five or six shipments of Jiangyin rice. In the market transactions, rural gangs purchased 500 dan. Top-quality goods barely maintained the original price, while the price of the middle and second grades decreased by three chi. The early indica rice from the south road was fine in grain, and although the arrival of green, thin indica rice and Shipu goods was small, the trading was extremely light, so the price decreased by two chi. The arrival and sales of Lu Yang sharp rice and glutinous rice were evenly matched, and the price did not rise or fall. The arrival of new japonica rice was brisk but sales were sluggish, so the price fell by about half a yuan.

Bean Noodle Market: Morning Drop, Afternoon Rebound 192

Yesterday, after the opening of the bean noodle market in the morning, the prices of each month's contract saw another huge drop. Because there was no major change in the quoted price of foreign wheat, and after the Wanguo Relief Wheat was confirmed, domestic long positions seemed to have lost hope for future sales in the disaster area. Furthermore, the factory's reserves are enough to last until February of next year. For these reasons, sentiment was greatly softened, and people rushed to sell, causing this month's contract to drop to a low of 2 liang and 05 fen and a half, October to 2 liang and 07 fen, November to 2 liang and 08 fen and 7.5 li, and December to 2 liang and 09. The 12th month's contract to 2 liang and 09 fen and 7.5 li. Amidst the severe floods, this degree of decline is good news for the future of food. In the afternoon, each contract rebounded by about 2 fen in the near term and 1 fen in the far term due to strong short covering. However, if actual sales do not pick up, it will still be difficult to stabilize the market. (The total daily transaction volume reached over 2.5 million bags.) As a result, this month's contract fell by 1 fen compared to the previous weekend, October fell by 7.5 li, November fell by 5 li, and December to February fell by 7.5 li.

Yesterday's futures wheat market showed a generally flat and weak trend in each month's contract after the opening in the morning and afternoon. Looking ahead, because the decline in the past few days has been huge, it may be necessary to consolidate temporarily. As a result, this month's contract fell by 2 fen compared to the previous day, October by 2 fen, November fell by 1 fen, December fell by 2 fen, January fell by 1 fen, and February remained unchanged. Southern and Northern Goods: Euryale Ferox Rises to 32 Taels 194

Euryale Ferox The market price has been rising steadily recently due to the shortage of inventory. For example, the top-quality southern Euryale Ferox has a market price of 160 yuan, but the goods are already out of stock. The price of pond-grown Euryale Ferox was less than 20 taels when it was at a low price, but now it has risen to 32 taels due to the scarcity of goods, which is also a rare high price in recent years. The market will not ease until new goods arrive in large quantities.

Silk and Tea: Hangzhou Area Autumn Silkworm Harvest is Unlikely 195

Purely Due to the Damage from Continuous Rain and Cold Weather, the Silkworms are Found to be Jaundiced

Farmers in various counties in the Hangzhou area mostly supplemented by raising autumn silkworms this year to compensate for the losses of the spring and summer cocoons. The amount of silkworm eggs raised was quite high. After the silkworms hatched, the weather was sunny and smooth, and the development was quite smooth. However, wind and rain caused trouble in the middle of the third sleep, and the silkworms suffered heavy damage. Now, the continuous autumn rains and sudden cold weather have caused most of the silkworms with vigorous appetites to become jaundiced, vomit black, and die by 60%. The autumn silkworm harvest this year is bound to be poor.

Gongxi Green Tea: Russian Sales Improve 196

Yesterday, the Russian Aid Society's interest in purchasing Gongxi green tea from Lai Lu Zhuang turned brisk. Hua Tea, Kechang, Qianyi, and other firms also started searching and purchasing in large numbers. The transaction was quite lively, and the market price also rose by 1-2 taels compared to last week. Core-extracted Zhenmei green tea continued to trend firm in the market. Needle tea and pearl tea were also sold as soon as they arrived. The green tea market was very firm. However, Qi Ning black tea had a full English demand, and Russian companies would not buy it unless it was cheap. The market still had more falls than rises.

Announcement 220

Mr. Xiao, Baiyun, Su Ling, Zhu Gongpu, Qianli, Zan, Mansheng, Jin Peishan, Tiehua, Li Xiufen, Chun, Deming, Fulan, Deren, You Chen, Yuxi, Li Zunquan, Bingqian, Lin, Doumei, Junshan, Zhu Yuxiang, Wan, Wang Bingqian, Guangmei, Shaqing, Li Chunsen, Ke, Junshan, Gentlemen, the manuscript fees for July have been settled. Please sign and stamp and collect them from the Accounting Department.

Guidelines for Book and Newspaper Introduction Manuscripts 221

(1) The text should be limited to introducing the latest publications from home and abroad. In addition to literary works, all books and newspapers on politics, economics, law, science, education, etc. are included in the introduction, but boring books and newspapers will not be introduced.

(2) The pictures should be limited to the latest works of new domestic and foreign artists and related illustrations.

(3) Articles on textual research or research on ancient Chinese books will not be published.

(4) Pictures and photos should be limited to those related to the text.

(5) Each article should not exceed 3,000 characters at most.

(6) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(7) Do not use blue ink to draw pictures, and do not use colored paper. White paper and black drawings must be used.

(8) Please indicate "Book and Newspaper Introduction Editorial Office" for incoming manuscripts.

(9) Incoming manuscripts will not be returned whether they are published or not. If a return is required, please declare in advance and attach sufficient postage stamps.

(10) Remuneration: 3

Business News 222

▲ Jingyi Xuan Dental Clinic announces: Teeth are related to a person's health. Our clinic has specially appointed a specialist director of dental medicine to preside over the operations. We are located opposite the Sino-Western Pharmacy in the Maijia Circle on Fourth Road. For inlays and crowns, whether porcelain or gold, we select only the best materials. Tooth extractions and fillings are performed using scientific methods, making them indistinguishable from natural teeth. Once fitted, they will never fall out or cause discomfort. To celebrate our opening, we are offering special low prices to show our appreciation to patrons.

▲ Yi'an Ju announces: The golden breeze sweeps away the summer heat, and the Mid-Autumn Festival is approaching. Mooncakes are now in season. The mooncakes made by our store at the Nanjing Road and Shilu intersection are already famous in Shanghai. Mr. Pan, the proprietor, has observed the increasing number of mooncake makers in the market. To maintain our past reputation, we have been particularly diligent this year in selecting various fillings and ingredients, even if it means higher costs. We are selecting top-quality materials for making the cakes and have hired many skilled artisans. The proprietor personally oversees the production. The weight and composition have both been increased, and there are even more varieties, totaling over thirty. Since being launched on the market, buyers...differently able to make real progress from those merely paying lip service to promotion.

▲ Yonghua Department Store, located at the Xinxiao intersection on Avenue Edward VII in the French Concession, announces: Our company weaves its own domestically produced silk fabrics, various threads and silk stockings, makes custom-tailored clothes, and gathers novel department store goods from various countries, as well as the latest styles of felt, silk and velvet hats. To show our appreciation to our customers, we are holding a special markdown sale for three weeks.

Theater News 223

▲ Xiaoximen Popular Lecture Hall announces: At 8 PM on the 5th, our hall held a costume lecture meeting. Over three hundred people attended. The chairman was Wang Longchao, and the recorder was Ni Zhizhan. The meeting proceeded as follows: (1) Wang Longchao lectured on the severity of this year's flood and urged the public to generously donate to disaster relief. (2) Wang Yinren and Cai Wenqing presented a comedic dialogue. (3) The costume lecture was titled "Overseas Cries," depicting the brutal killings of overseas Chinese by Koreans, exposing the insidious schemes of the Japanese, and aimed at awakening the public to unanimously oppose Japan and aid overseas Chinese. The audience applauded, showing that everyone has a responsibility for the survival of the nation. Our hall holds regular lectures, which were suspended due to the summer vacation but have now resumed their original schedule.

▲ Imperial Grand Theater announces: Wang Meiyu's performance of reformed new drama at the Imperial Grand Theater opened yesterday. Before 8 PM, it was already sold out. The first performance was "The Sentimental Dancing Girl," with each scene lively and striving for perfection. Prominent Shanghai figures such as Du Yuesheng presented silver shields, plaques, and other items. We heard that the audience was too crowded yesterday, leading to many casual and careless handling of ticket sales and reception. We will strive to correct this in the future and strive for perfection.

Medical News 224

▲ The Hongkou Branch of Baohe Tang on North Sichuan Road announces: Since our opening, our business has been quite prosperous. The various raw and processed medicinal materials, pills, powders, plasters, and elixirs we sell are all top-quality products, and our prices are extremely fair. We open at 7 AM every morning and have hired multiple national doctors to provide free consultations on a rotating basis throughout the day, without charging any fees. We also fill prescriptions for customers, prepare and deliver medicine, regardless of distance. A phone call will immediately dispatch someone to come. We have rickshaws for transportation, making it very convenient and providing complete service without charging any labor fees.

▲ Renowned Shaoxing doctor Xie Enhao announces: I, Dr. Xie, have a long family tradition of medical expertise and specialize in treating typhoid fever, hemoptysis, pediatrics, gynecology, etc., and I can invariably bring about recovery. I have now come to Shanghai for consultations and have established a clinic at 648 Tianjin Road, telephone number 61247. For the poor and sick, I will generally waive consultation fees.
